Executive Yuan Resolves to Appoint Li Pingheng and Others as Representatives to the International Labor Conference

Yu Jiaji Appointed Secretary-General of the Beiping Political Reorganization Committee

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan held its 199th meeting at 9:00 a.m. on the 12th. Those present were Wang Zhaoming, Chen Gongbo, Wang Shijie, Zhu Jiahua, Shi Qingyang, Chen Shuren, Liu Ruiheng, Chu Minyi, Peng Xuepei, Gan Naiguang, Tang Youren, Fu Rulin, Xu Mo, Cao Haosen, Chen Jiliang, Chen Xunyong, Zou Lin, Qin Fen, Liu Weichi, Duan Xipeng, Zeng Zhongming, etc., chaired by President Wang.

(A) Reporting Matters

President's Report: The late Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, Lu Diping, engaged in revolution, with remarkable military achievements. Subsequently leading the territory, also with comforting benefits. In total, his life was honest and unyielding. Governing the military and politics, for twenty years. No great savings at home, especially difficult for recent people. Now hearing of his death, deeply mourn his loss. The Yuan has submitted to the National Government, for generous posthumous commendations, clear orders issued, and providing funeral expenses of 5,000 yuan.

(B) Reviewing Reports

(I) Minister of Foreign Affairs and Concurrent Minister Wang, Minister of Military Affairs He, Minister of the Navy Chen, Acting Minister of Interior Gan reported on the case of submitting for review the Regulations for the Management of the Red Cross Society, which was revised by the four ministries of Interior, Foreign Affairs, Military Affairs, and Navy. The draft amendment has been slightly revised, and the amendment is submitted for your approval. Resolution: Passed and communicated to the Legislative Yuan.

(II) Minister of Foreign Affairs and Concurrent Minister Wang, Minister of Military Affairs He, Minister of the Navy Chen, Minister of Industry Chen, Minister of Communications Zhu, Minister of Railways Gu, Acting Minister of Interior Gan reported on the case of submitting for review the draft Factory Safety and Sanitation Regulations submitted by the Ministry of Industry. The original draft regulations have been revised, and the amendment is submitted for your approval. Resolution: Revised and passed, communicated to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation.

(III) Minister of Finance Kong, Acting Minister of Interior Gan reported on the case of submitting for review the Provisional Regulations for Land Registration in Fujian Province, which has been revised, for your approval. Resolution: Passed.

(C) Appointments and Removals

(I) Minister of Finance Kong submitted that Kou Xia, a member of the Shaanxi Donation and Tax Supervision Committee, has repeatedly requested to resign. All vacancies should be filled as soon as possible. Checking the previously submitted list, there is Fan Zidong, a Shaanxi elder, currently serving as the president of the Yisu Society. Can he be appointed to fill the vacancy? Please approve the order. Resolution: Passed.

(II) Minister of Finance Kong submitted that Shi Wei, director of the Hebei Stamp Tax and Tobacco and Alcohol Bureau, Cao Mingxian, deputy director of the Hubei Stamp Tax and Tobacco and Alcohol Bureau, and Zeng Luda, director of the Changsha Sub-District Unified Tax Management Office of the Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi area, are awaiting other appointments. Xu Xian, deputy director of the Fujian Stamp Tax and Tobacco and Alcohol Bureau, has other appointments. Please remove them from their positions. Also, the Hebei Finance Special Commissioner's Office, which has been abolished, Ning Chengen, the original special commissioner, should be removed from his position. Also, please appoint Ding Chungao as director of the Hebei Stamp Tax and Tobacco and Alcohol Bureau, Ning Chengen as director of the Hebei-Chahar-Suiyuan Unified Tax Bureau, Yang Duo as deputy director of the Hubei Stamp Tax and Alcohol Bureau, Wang Guanghui as deputy director of the Fujian Stamp Tax and Tobacco and Alcohol Bureau, Guan Jiyu as deputy director of the Hebei-Chahar-Suiyuan Unified Tax Bureau, and Nie Qifan as director of the Changsha Sub-District Unified Tax Management Office of the Hunan-Hubei-Jiangxi area. Resolution: Passed.

(III) Minister of Military Affairs He submitted that Huang Hanxun, commander of the 76th Brigade of the 26th Division of the Army, has resigned due to illness. It is proposed to reappoint him as a Major General Councilor of the Military Council. Resolution: Passed.

(IV) Minister of Military Affairs He submitted that Chen Qizhi, director of the General Affairs Department of the Training Supervision Department, has other appointments. It is proposed to remove him from his position. The vacancy is proposed to be filled by Zang Zhuo, a Lieutenant General Councilor of the Military Council and concurrent director of the General Affairs Department. The vacancy in the General Affairs Department of the Military Council is proposed to be filled by Li Er Kang. Resolution: Passed.

(V) Minister of Military Affairs He requested the appointment of Wang Wenxian as Chief of Staff of the 27th Division of the Army and Ge Tingjun as Commander of the 80th Brigade of Infantry of the Division. Resolution: Passed.

(VI) Chairman Huang of the Beiping Political Affairs Reorganization Committee submitted that He Qigong, the Secretary-General of the Committee, has requested to resign due to illness. It is requested to approve the resignation and appoint Yu Jiaji to fill the vacancy. Resolution: Passed.

(D) Discussion Matters

(I) Minister of Foreign Affairs and Concurrent Minister Wang submitted a proposal to re-divide the inspection areas and to formulate provisional regulations for the inspection commissioner's office. Please approve the record. Resolution: Revised and passed, approved for the record.

(II) Acting Minister of Interior Gan requested to revise Article 4, Item 6 of the Provisional Organizational Charter of the Food Transportation and Sales Bureau, "Matters of assessing local storage" to "Matters of investigating local granaries." Resolution: Passed, revised to "Matters of investigating local storage."

(III) Acting Minister of Interior Gan, Chairman Liu of the Anti-Opium Committee, jointly submitted that the Zhejiang Provincial Anti-Drug Association's urgent telegram for the outstanding achievements of Lu Bichou, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, in prohibiting opium. It is requested to commend him generously in accordance with the Regulations on Anti-Opium Performance. It is proposed to submit it to the National Government, following precedent, to grant a clear commendation to encourage meritorious service. Resolution: Submit to the National Government to grant a clear commendation.

(IV) Minister of Industry Chen proposed that Li Pingheng be appointed as the first government representative, Bao Huaguo as the second representative, to attend the 19th International Labor Conference. Luo Shian is the advisor to the government representative, Yang Deqiao is the secretary to the government representative. Please vote for a decision. Resolution: Passed. (12th Central News Agency Telegram)

Liu Xiang Rectifies Officialdom

(Chongqing) Liu Xiang issued a general order yesterday to all county magistrates to rectify the officialdom, with three admonitions: (I) Should implement care for the people, and strictly prohibit harsh and trivial disturbances. (II) Each county magistrate should actively seek progress. (III) Each county magistrate, receiving salary, should encourage honesty and integrity. (12th Central News Agency Telegram)

Zhang Dongsun Arrives in Guangdong Under Orders from Wang and Sun

(Hong Kong) Zhang Dongsun arrived in Guangdong under orders from Wang and Sun to discuss important matters with Chen and Li. After completing twelve matters, he will come to Hong Kong and return north. (12th Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Jiang Bocheng returned to the province from Hong Kong on the 11th with his family, and Huang Renhuan left the province on the 11th to return to his defense. (12th Dispatch)

Huang Musong Leaves Hong Kong for the North This Morning

(Hong Kong) The Hong Kong Chongzheng Association held a meeting at 8:00 p.m. on the 12th to welcome Huang Musong. Huang left Hong Kong for the north on the Asia Queen at 6:00 a.m. on the 13th. (12th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Nanjing) Huang Musong's staff member Gao Changzhu said: (I) Huang was dispatched to Tibet this time to confer titles and pay respects to the Dalai Lama, which was well received by all Tibetan officials, people, monks, and laity. (II) The Tibetan side expressed that they would immediately dispatch personnel to Nanjing to thank them when Huang left Tibet, but no telegram has been received to date. Who will come to Nanjing and when they will depart are unknown. (III) Huang is coming north from Hong Kong on the Asia Queen on the 13th, and will arrive in Shanghai on the morning of the 16th, and then go to Nanjing. (12th Dispatch)

Japanese Fleet Commander Hyakutake Visits Hong Kong Governor

(Hong Kong) Japanese Third Fleet Commander Hyakutake visited Hong Kong Governor Peel at the Governor's Mansion at 10:00 a.m. on the 12th. Peel also paid a return visit to the Kuma cruiser at 11:00 a.m. Hyakutake is scheduled to enter the province on the 13th to visit the Guangdong authorities. (12th Central News Agency Telegram)

Guangdong Fleet Discusses Methods to Search and Suppress Pirates

Fan Yongjiang, a robber from the Tongzhou Steamer, Confesses to the Robbery

(Hong Kong) Guangdong Fleet Commander Zhang Zhiying summoned Cai Tenghui, the special agent chief of the Marine Corps stationed in Dapeng Bay, on the 12th to discuss methods to search and suppress pirates. It was decided to send troops within a month to completely wipe out the pirates along the coast of the bay. (12th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Hong Kong) A robber from the Tongzhou Steamer, Fan Yongjiang, was captured in Fanhegang, Huizhou, and escorted to the province on the 12th. According to his confession, there are still ten people at large. (12th Dispatch)

(Guangzhou) It is now known that the Magistrate of Huiyang County personally led the police to search for the bandits who robbed the Tongzhou Steamer and arrested one Fan. It is heard that Fan and three accomplices escaped with the stolen goods on a small fishing boat near Haifeng that day. Several other companions landed near the lighthouse, each carrying stolen goods worth 30 yuan, 200 yuan of unsigned Bank of China banknotes, and a pistol. According to Fan's confession, there were a total of ten accomplices who gathered in Haifeng on January 17th. The next morning, they took a train to Shantou, and the following day, they departed on the Yuezhou Steamer. They arrived in Shanghai on the 24th, staying at the Ping'an Hotel for several days to discuss a plan to rob a ship. Later, they disguised themselves as passengers and boarded the Tongzhou Steamer together, robbing a total of 1,300 yuan in foreign banknotes, five boxes of unsigned Bank of China banknotes, coats, fur coats, and several blankets. They also found 19 pistols on the Tongzhou Steamer and killed two foreign crew members. As for the bandit leader Fang, he has not been arrested yet. Fan is from Feng, with Dapeng Bay as his lair. (12th Reuters Telegram)

Minnan Militia, Zhan's Unit, to be Reorganized

(Xiamen) The Minnani Militia that have not been organized include: Anxi Zhan Fangzhen, Guo Zong, Lu Zhenshan, Wu Yinshi, Wang Chaofu, Changtai Ye Wenlong, Pinghe You Liutian, Hui'an Wang Zhenan, Zhu Geqiu Nine major groups. Those who have requested organization from the Pacification Headquarters are Zhan, Guo, Lu, You, Ye. Except that Zhan has been approved for reorganization, the rest are awaiting discussion between the Pacification Headquarters and the Provincial Government. Tian Xiyuan, Chief of Staff of the Pacification Headquarters, Zheng Bingru, Security Department Staff, will depart for Anxi tomorrow if the weather is clear to verify Zhan's unit. (12th Dispatch)

(Xiamen) Chen Qi, Commander of the 80th Division stationed in Zhangzhou, is scheduled to convene a Zhangzhou Pacification Conference in Zhangzhou on the 15th, notifying military and government officials of all counties to attend. (12th Dispatch)

(Xiamen) Recently, a telegram from Quanzhou reported that Guo Zong's militia in Anxi are disturbing the people in the southern district. The Pacification Headquarters ordered Dou Changqing's regiment to encircle and suppress them. Brigade Commander Xie Fusan went to Xiping to command. (12th Dispatch)

Central Army Pursues and Suppresses Along the Xugu Line

Liu Wenhui Sends Troops to Deploy Along the Jinsha River

Remnants of Bandits in Guizhou Flee to Jianwu

Xue Yue Orders Various Units to Intercept

(Chongqing) Xue Yue's First and Second Pursuit Brigades arrived in Gulin on the 8th, capturing many along the way. On the 9th, they continued to pursue and suppress along the Xugu Line. The Third and Fourth Pursuit Brigades also plan to pursue and suppress along the Xugu Line. The Second and Fourth Columns led by Zhou Dai's command post are also advancing in the same direction. (12th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Chongqing) Liu Wenhui sent Liu Yuanxun and Xu Jianshuang's brigades to deploy along the upper reaches of the Jinsha River and the areas along the Jianghe and Yanyuan Rivers.

(Changsha) A telegram from Cili said that a portion of Xiao He's bandit group is entrenched in Xikou, building fortifications, attempting to obstruct our army's advance and suppression. On the afternoon of the 10th, our Guo Division's Wang Brigade and Li Division's Tao Chen Brigades advanced from Laoyakou Sanxingdu and other places, attacking the bandits from both sides. The bandits suffered heavy losses and fled to the Houxi Liangshan. Also, Chen Quzhen's unit of the New 34th Division defeated more than a thousand bandits near Yongshun City on the 3rd. Due to excessive casualties, the bandits fled towards Fu's Jiazhai Tawo at night. A portion of the bandits contacted more than a thousand bandits near Daqingshan Guanfangwan Shidi West in Yong on the 4th. Fighting fiercely from dawn to dusk, the bandits collapsed due to internal changes and fled towards Sangzhi. (12th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Chongqing) A telegram from Guiyang on the 11th said that Xue Yue telegraphed that the bandits fled to Jianwu. He has ordered Zhou and Wang's columns and the Luo Xie and Li units to rush to that area to contact the Sichuan army and annihilate the bandits in the area east of the Hengjiang and Jinsha Rivers. (12th Central News Agency Telegram)

(Chongqing) Approximately 40,000 to 50,000 remnants of Zhu Mao's bandits sneaked near Chishui on the Sichuan-Guizhou border and were defeated by the Sichuan army, splitting into two routes and fleeing towards Yunnan Province. Loan Conditions of Various Banks in Beijing

(Nanjing) It has recently been rumored that banks in Beijing have received a notice from the Shanghai head office regarding mortgage loans for immovable property, stating that they will temporarily cease to operate this business. In fact, this is not universal. According to a bank source, the situation of real estate mortgages in Beijing is that in the past, banks in Beijing operated housing mortgages in a prudent manner, which was not the main part of their business. To meet social needs, they carefully issued loans based on collateral and guarantees to provide turnover for all sectors. According to the regulations of the Ministry of Finance, commercial banks are not allowed to exclusively engage in housing mortgages, but they are allowed to concurrently operate property mortgages under the savings department of the savings section, with a maximum limit of six years to pay off principal and interest. The mortgage amount is generally 30% of the original value, with a monthly interest rate of about 1.2%, which is a very prudent investment and should not cause problems. (Special dispatch, 12th)

(Nanjing) The person in charge of Jin City Bank said that last year the Shanghai money market was extremely tight, and occasionally one or two banks tightened their lending, which was expected. However, there have been no such rumors in Beijing. According to the Beijing Bankers Association, the scope of real estate mortgages is also wider. The rumor that various banks have received a notice from the Shanghai head office to suspend this type of mortgage is not true. An investigation shows that most real estate mortgages in Beijing are for housing, and pure land without buildings is rarely accepted due to its lack of production, unless there is a special and reliable guarantee. In short, in a sluggish market, banks primarily focus on ensuring clear guarantees when accepting collateral and do not reject all mortgages. (Special dispatch, 12th)

Hirota Actively Pursues Diplomacy with China and Russia

Seeks Economic Development with China

Eases Tensions with Russia

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Hirota is formulating diplomatic strategies for the major current situation, aiming to actively adjust Sino-Japanese and Japanese-Russian relations in parallel with arms reduction countermeasures. He is currently preparing with the determination to personally take action. The reasons why Foreign Minister Hirota strongly advocates adjusting Sino-Japanese relations are as follows: 1. At the London Disarmament Preparatory Conference, Japan's proposals are far from those of Britain and the United States, making it difficult to approach. 2. The reason why Britain and the United States do not recognize Japan's request for equality is that they fear Japan's development toward China, Outer Mongolia, and Siberia. 3. Britain and the United States hope that Japan will clarify its attitude and dispel this concern. Therefore, although Foreign Minister Hirota will not hold an arms reduction broadcast after the return of the Japanese arms reduction representative, in order to stimulate the emotions of various countries,

China Policy - The Foreign Minister's attitude and policy toward China are as follows: 1. Abandon previous petty suspicions. Japan will definitely provide China with productive assistance. 2. Provide necessary human and material assistance to China, which is a raw material supply country. 3. Japan must seek raw materials from China, and China must purchase Japan's refined products, and establish a reciprocal trade agreement.

Russia Policy - His policy toward Russia is as follows: 1. Start direct negotiations between Japan and Russia, revise the fisheries and oil agreements, and persuade the establishment of a Japan-"Manchukuo"-Russia border committee and a demilitarized zone. 2. If the Soviet Union understands Japan's sincerity, it will persuade it to expand the demilitarized zone and withdraw military facilities east of Lake Baikal. If the Soviet Union recognizes this, Japan will also agree to limit Japan's military deployment in northern Manchuria in order to completely eliminate international disputes between Japan-"Manchukuo"-Russia. As for the specific negotiations with China and Russia, the starting date will be after Ambassador Arima returns to China at the end of March, and for Russia, it will be after Ambassador Ota, who is returning home, assumes office in March. (Dentsu dispatch, 12th)

Centered on Commercial Counselor Yokotake, an important consultation was held on concrete measures to establish Sino-Japanese economic cooperation. Commercial Counselor Yokotake's concrete measures are stated as follows:

1. Fundamentally, China must rely on its own efforts. Therefore, Japan must hire technicians to improve the cultivation methods of rice, wheat, cotton, etc., in order to reduce imports and increase exports. Because Japan alone has the potential to import 100 million gold worth of cotton, an improvement in trade may be realized. 2. There must be a thorough end to anti-Japanese sentiment, and people must realize that cheap and high-quality Japanese goods are definitely effective for China's self-reliance. 3. However, the current Chinese economy is on the verge of collapse and must be rescued. Therefore, it is necessary to lend money to China. Commercial Counselor Yokotake also made the same remarks to Foreign Minister Hirota in the afternoon. (Dentsu dispatch, 12th)

US Reinforces National Defense Plan

Building an Invincible Merchant Fleet

Strengthening Coastal Defense Works

(Washington) News from reliable sources today indicates that the government is currently planning to reinforce the national defense plan, which is divided into three points: ㈠ strengthening the merchant fleet; ㈡ strengthening coastal defense works; ㈢ reforming aviation bases. News of the strengthening of the merchant fleet was announced simultaneously with news of the current plan for an invincible merchant fleet. It is said that President Roosevelt had previously commissioned former Attorney General under President Wilson, Balmore, to draft a bill to enable the Navy to have the cooperation of a strong merchant fleet in the event of an incident. It is learned that Balmore has held meetings with officials of the Shipping Bureau for several weeks and has now formulated a plan to abolish postal subsidies and directly pay subsidies to American shipping companies. The bill will soon be submitted to Congress, it is said. Congress may also soon accept the Budget Committee's recommendation to allocate 20 to 30 million yuan from the 300,000,000 yuan public works budget for the construction of warships. As for naval expenditures, 4 million yuan may be proposed for the construction of floating docks at Pearl Harbor and the Pacific Ocean naval base, and it is also possible to build naval floating dock projects in Bremerton, Washington, with the same amount. It is said that the naval budget also includes the following plans: 3.5 million yuan for the construction of new-style projects at the Pensacola Naval Training Station, which has the largest aviation base in the country; ㈡ 120,000 yuan for the equipment of the Mare Island Naval Shipyard ordnance depot in San Francisco; ㈢ 100,000 yuan for the construction of the San Nicolas Air Station in California; ㈣ a radio station in St. Paul, Alaska; ㈤ 500,000 yuan for new-style equipment at the Hawaiian aviation base; ㈥ 500,000 yuan for the expansion of the submarine base in Coco Solo, Panama Canal Zone; ㈦ 800,000 yuan for the Coco Solo submarine and aviation base. Congressman Routt and Tumult also asked the House Army Committee to consolidate the defenses of the Pacific Northwest coast and Alaska. Routt said that Washington should have an aviation base, and that the entire state of Washington has no anti-aircraft artillery. Tumult said that Alaska is the proper route from Yokohama to the United States, and that if the East attacks the United States, it will undoubtedly abandon the southern route and take the route through Alaska. Therefore, although I support the defense works on the island of Hawaii, I feel that Alaska is more in need of this equipment. (Eleventh National Telegram)

US Army Chief of Staff Advocates for Naval Supremacy

Army and Air Force Should Be Expanded Simultaneously

Draft Plan Divided into Three Sections

Chicago – US Army Chief of Staff Bellgreno today drafted a military plan divided into three sections, one of which advocates that the United States build the most superior navy. Bellgreno also advocates that the United States actively carry out an exclusion movement. His argument is as follows: If Europe needs communism, Hitlerism, or fascism, then it is free to do so, but the United States does not need it. The United States can only accommodate Americans and American ideas. Bell's defense plan is purely defensive in nature. Bell said that the geographical location of the United States and its position in international debt should give the United States the most superior navy stipulated in the London Naval Treaty. Therefore, the United States should immediately build ships to the extent permitted by the treaty. The United States should also have a standing army whose training and equipment can be compared with those of the great powers. The army should have sufficient soldiers and munitions to defend the coasts of the United States and defend against possible aggression. The third section of the unified plan stipulates the expansion of the current National Defense Force and the adoption of conscription, so that in the event of an incident, the people can take up arms against the enemy. Bell went on to say that the Air Force should also be increased. He expressed his approval of the plan to build an aviation base in Hawaii for 11 million yuan. The US Army also requested that Congress pass a bill to gather capital and manpower to avoid the dispersion of national strength and prohibit private individuals and companies from profiting during wartime so that there is no profit to be made from munitions, etc. (Eleventh National Telegram)

Saar Financial Power Returns to Germany; Franco-German Agreement Signed

Rome – Experts from France and Germany handling the transfer of power in the Saar region have already completed their work. The experts have drafted 28 draft agreements in Basel, Switzerland, all of which have been initialed. The three-person committee initially proposed combining these 28 agreements into one document, but later advocated combining them into three or four agreements. The first of these, concerning currency exchange and the tariff system, was officially signed in Rome yesterday. Among the various agreements, the most important is the general agreement on the transfer of jurisdiction over mines and railways. The mines and railways in the Saar region owned by France will be redeemed by Germany at a price in accordance with the resolution of December 3 last year. The price is set at 900 million francs. The issue of leased land is being discussed by representatives of France and Germany in Berlin and will be included in the agreement after a solution is agreed upon. In addition, there are agreements on French private insurance and social insurance in the Saar region. The amount of private insurance is quite large. Although social insurance was resolved by a treaty concluded between France and Germany in 1932, it has not been implemented. A new agreement is now being drafted so that this treaty can be implemented and take effect. As for the debt settlement method, it is currently being drafted, and its form has not yet been determined. After the transfer of power in the Saar, the francs used by the people must be exchanged for marks, but it is stipulated that those leaving the Saar region, such as French people, do not have to exchange them. This is more important for private individuals than for companies. In addition, German law stipulates that those residing in German territory should deposit their capital in the central bank, but this has not yet been implemented for foreigners. An agreement will now be drawn up separately for French people and those leaving the Saar to protect them from being subject to this type of law. (Twelfth Havas Telegram)

No Germs Ever Found in Chinese Eggs Imported to England

British Under-Secretary of Health Answers Member's Question

(London) At today's meeting of the House of Commons, Conservative MP Hurt asked whether the method of making Chinese liquid eggs meets sanitary conditions, whether it has been carefully inspected after entering England, and asked the British representative in China to conduct a thorough investigation. Under-Secretary of Health Shakespeare replied that there is no clear evidence regarding sanitary conditions, but it must be inspected when it is transported to various ports in England, and if it is not suitable for human consumption, it must be confiscated. The Ministry of Health has never found germs in this type of egg product, and a mold expert is now being hired to examine its samples, he said. Hurt also asked why such a huge amount of Chinese eggs is not subject to the sanitary precautions applied to British produce. Shakespeare did not answer. (Eleventh Reuters Telegram)

Current Affairs Commentary

On Promoting Afforestation with Caution

The Zhejiang Provincial Government plans to plant trees on both sides of the roads because more than 2,570 kilometers of roads have been built in Zhejiang Province in recent years. It is estimated that about 300,000 trees will be planted. In a passive sense, this is enough to consolidate the roadbed and add to the scenery along the road. In an active sense, it is enough to inspire interest in new construction. These trees will also have practical uses in the future.

China was originally a country with abundant natural resources and superior human efforts. However, since contacting other countries in the world in the past century, our abundant natural resources have not been developed, and our superior manual labor has also fallen behind. We have only relied on nature to maintain the face of an agricultural nation. Others have made progress of a thousand miles a day, but we have almost stagnated here. Even if there is some progress, it is very slow. The difference in speed is like the ratio of a bullock cart to an airplane. In such contrast, the strengths of our country's agriculture and handicrafts have gradually been submerged, and the scene of decline has become more obvious. For example, the production of wood is a by-product of agricultural countries, and at least it should be able to be self-sufficient. But the fact is just the opposite. The buildings in large cities, of course, use foreign imported wood, and even small and medium-sized cities also use foreign wood. This reflects that agricultural operators only care about current living gains and have no spare capacity to plan for slightly longer-term undertakings. I am afraid that the actual poverty situation in China is more than that. Many famous mountains and scenic spots, such as the mountains around West Lake in Hangzhou, and on Putuo Island, do not necessarily lack the financial resources to engage in tree planting, nor do they lack open space for planting. However, many mountains have become colorless barren mountains. Occasionally, due to the opportunity of some birds, one or two trees grow as decorations for the scenery, which is actually not very helpful. It is also not good for the overall mountain scenery. In the rainy season, if the rainfall is slightly more, floods will occur. If the rainfall is slightly less, there will be a shortage of drought and little room for turnover adjustment. The moisture contained in the ground decreases. If this continues for a long time, there is a danger of turning into a desert. This phenomenon is particularly obvious along the Longhai Railway from Shangqiu to Zhongmou.

In recent years, the whole country has gradually understood the need to promote afforestation. It is not only to decorate the scenery, but also has a great relationship with agricultural cultivation and climate regulation. Therefore, the promotion of afforestation is well known throughout the country, and some places have indeed made efforts to plant many trees. However, afforestation is a very common thing to say, and everyone has no doubts that more should be planted. It is just that when implementing it, many difficult problems immediately arise. ㈠ At present, the most common situation for farmers who cultivate the land is that there are many people and little land. The land will not increase, but the number of people eating is increasing day by day. Therefore, they want to develop land power as much as possible, regardless of the fact that trees that do not see benefits in the eyes block their hot land for production. ㈡ Although farmers are conservative, they have no time to plan for long-term facilities during the period when their lives are not yet stable. Therefore, they are not only not enthusiastic about afforestation, but also sometimes destroy existing trees. ㈢ In the present situation where the locality has exhausted its people's strength and the people are tired, even if they intend to afforest, there is no way to start. Because the source of seedlings is lacking, and there is even no financial capacity to purchase them. ㈣ Because of inconvenient transportation, even if there are trees all over the mountains in more remote places, there is no way to transport them. Moreover, the taxes are heavy, and they cannot help but hesitate. The appeal of Jianmu merchants reported in today's newspaper is due to the heavy taxes. Now the whole country knows that letting trees "grow naturally" is not a solution. Moreover, "growing naturally" takes a very long time. Therefore, proper cultivation is a necessary thing at present. The tree cultivation method should be discussed by specialists in terms of technology. Today, I will only talk about the general situation. First, we must eliminate man-made destruction so that most farmers know the importance of afforestation. Second, all public barren mountains should be planned and planted by local governments, and plants suitable for the soil of the area should be selected. It is also necessary to estimate how long it will take to harvest once after a certain period to remove the old and bring forth the new. There must also be a plan for what the use is. Even if the effect is to be achieved ten or twenty years or even longer, the intangible regulation of the climate and the tangible special income are also huge benefits. Therefore, we believe that the afforestation movement should be spread throughout the country, especially in mountainous areas.

Italy Presses Abyssinia with Military and Diplomatic Advances

Five Harsh Demands to Atti

Compensation and Apology, Respect for the Italian Flag

Italian Troops Mobilize Awaiting Opportunity to Attack

Abyssinians Resolve on Final Resistance

(Rome) At this time of dense war clouds in the Italo-Abyssinian War, Italy has made five demands of Atti: ㈠ Abyssinia must compensate Italy for its losses, reportedly set at one million gold pounds; ㈡ The Abyssinian government must formally apologize; ㈢ An Abyssinian must be sent to pay respects to the Italian flag; ㈣ An Italo-Abyssinian border commission must be organized; ㈤ Abyssinians must not violate the Italian border. News of these five demands was transmitted simultaneously with news that the Italian government has appointed General Graziani as commander of the Abyssinian expeditionary force. Graziani has put down the rebellion of the Libyan natives and has experience in dealing with colonial peoples. Recently, he also led troops to garrison the Austrian border. Italian sources say that there are about 30,000 Abyssinian troops gathering on the Italian border. (Twelfth National Telegram)

Another Telegram – At the same time as this Italo-Abyssinian War, mobilization is in full swing, and diplomatic methods are also being adopted, such as Italy's demand for compensation for losses, which is one aspect. This kind of negotiation can turn the situation towards moderation and open a way to resolve the dispute. It is said that the League of Nations has appointed a mixed commission to establish a reasonable boundary on the Italo-Abyssinian border to avoid future unfortunate events. (Twelfth National Telegram)

(Rome) The Abyssinian chargé d'affaires in Italy told Reuters today that if Italy wants to start a war with Abyssinia, Abyssinia intends to defend its territory to the last man. Abyssinia has an armed force of 800,000 men and can recruit another 1 million men. Abyssinia has weapons of the new era, but lacks tanks and aircraft. It is heard that 40,000 Italian troops have been stationed in Eritrea. The Italian government announced today that negotiations to resolve the dispute are currently underway in the Abyssinian capital. (Eleventh Reuters Telegram)

Abyssinia – Here, due to the Italian mobilization, soldiers in mountain forts have recently begun test-firing rifles to cope with the Italian invasion. It is said that 50,000 to 80,000 troops have been mobilized to cope with the Italian army, all equipped with new weapons and machine guns. At the same time, the Italian mobilization has made the international situation serious. Abyssinian soldiers are accustomed to highland life and are brave and fierce. In the end, Italy may win, but things are not as simple as expected, because it is now the rainy season and it is very inconvenient for large teams to march. However, Italy continues to mobilize, so the air of war is quite strong. (Eleventh National Telegram)

(Rome) It is now believed that the Italian government will still try to avoid opening hostilities with Abyssinia. Today, the official explanation for the mobilization of two army divisions is that Abyssinia is currently garrisoning 30,000 troops on the border and can continue to send 100,000 more. Italy has no choice but to prepare reinforcements to defend its colonies and take steps to avoid further border conflicts. The authorities also said that the two divisions mobilized, one stationed in Florence and one stationed in Messina, totaling 30,000 troops, are ready to attack Abyssinia when necessary. The Abyssinian chargé d'affaires in Rome went to the Italian Foreign Ministry this afternoon to discuss this matter. (Eleventh Reuters Telegram)

(Rome) Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has protested to Abyssinia, roughly saying that Italy has reached the end of its tolerance. If diplomacy cannot fully satisfy Italy, then Italy is ready to fight on the border between Abyssinia and Italian Somaliland. According to government explanations, Italy believes that the Abyssinian guerrillas who have repeatedly attacked the Italian army in recent times must be thoroughly eliminated, and there are many armed troops on the Abyssinian border, and these soldiers have also repeatedly disturbed border security. Mussolini has been greatly shocked, because these current situations are not overstated. The Political Council has been extremely calm, but it must now be thoroughly resolved. According to Abyssinian news, officials in the country do not believe that Italy can take the offensive at this time of year, as it is extremely difficult to march across the border. Although diplomatic relations are very tense now, officials still hope that war can be avoided. As for Italy, it pays no attention to the climate issue, because if decisive measures are not taken again, border disturbances will never end. Therefore, the army has been prepared and can depart at any time. However, even if war breaks out, it is feared that Italy, like Japan in Manchuria and the United States in Nicaragua, will not formally declare war, and Mussolini's army will directly occupy Abyssinian territory to await the end of the event, until the Italian government is satisfied. The Abyssinian army is also quite large, and if forced to, it may try its best to resist. Observers say that this kind of resistance is difficult to sustain under the heavy artillery, tanks, and other sophisticated weapons. (Eleventh National Telegram)

Abyssinian Military Equipment Situation

(Rome) A military magazine called "Military Power" recently published the situation of the Abyssinian military equipment. According to reports, the Abyssinian army is composed of several armed teams, some of which are directly under the Abyssinian emperor and some of which belong to local leaders. Thirty percent of the country's people can be mobilized, totaling 2 million people, but only 500,000 people have weapons. The types of weapons are of varying quality, but new-style portable machine guns have also been deployed. The artillery has a total of 180 cannons, in addition to 250 machine guns, six tanks, and more than ten aircraft. (Eleventh Havas Telegram)

Truth About Italian Military Mobilization

(Rome) The Italo-Abyssinian conflict has been going on for a long time, and now it has only been made public. At the same time, the actual date of the Italian mobilization and the date of the announcement are also very different. This method has aroused various rumors in political circles here. Some say that the truth of the whole facts is not as it is, and some say that not only the reservists born in 1911 have been mobilized, but also those born from 1908 to 1912 have been mobilized. Some say that all combat personnel have been mobilized, and some of them will be sent overseas in one or two days. Although it is still difficult to know the truth, the general public believes that Italy is determined to take large-scale action against Abyssinia to make Abyssinia submit. However, now it is the rainy season, and it is feared that a bad war will not occur. (Twelfth National Telegram)

League of Nations Uneasy

(Geneva) The League of Nations today suddenly felt the seriousness of the conflict between Italy and Abyssinia, because Italian Prime Minister Mussolini mobilized troops, preparing to attack the Abyssinians and attack the defense line between Italian Somaliland and Ethiopia. It is now believed that the League of Nations Executive Council, which will meet at the end of this month to monitor the return of the Saar to Germany, may be forced to intervene in the Italo-Abyssinian conflict. Abyssinia may become the second "Manchukuo," and key figures are very uneasy. (Twelfth National Telegram)

England Mediates

(London) Regarding the rumor that Italy sent an ultimatum to the government of Abyssinia, officials here claimed this evening that it has not been confirmed. Britain is still mediating between the two governments to conduct direct negotiations to clarify the border between Italian territories in East Africa and Abyssinia. If so, various other outstanding issues will naturally be easier to resolve. (Eleventh Havas Telegram)

(London) Regarding the conflict between Italian troops and Abyssinian troops, the British government ordered its ambassador to Italy, Sir Drummond, to inquire about the news. According to Drummond's report, the Italian government has prepared two infantry divisions equipped with wartime personnel, that is, 35,000 people, but stated that this move is purely a precautionary measure. Drummond told the Italian government that he hoped that Italy could begin negotiations with Abyssinia in the near future, in accordance with the recommendation of the League of Nations Executive Council in January of this year, to resolve the dispute. (Twelfth Havas Telegram)

Germany Will Issue a Reply to the Anglo-French Proposal Soon

Belgium Supports the Sky Pact

Formally Notifies the British Government

(Paris) Germany's reply to the Anglo-French agreement recently concluded in London is expected to be issued on Thursday. It is now believed that its wording must be vague, containing a request for negotiations, but not expressing the government's views. (Eleventh Reuters Telegram)

(Paris) The Berlin correspondent of the Petit Parisien predicted the content of Germany's reply to the Anglo-French London Agreement and published its outline as follows: "The Anglo-French Agreement is sufficient to guarantee the western border of Germany and is therefore supported, but the Danube Convention, especially the East European Mutual Assistance Pact, in the form drafted in Rome and London, is strongly opposed. Germany is unwilling to guarantee the eastern border of Soviet Russia with its military force, and is also unwilling to be involved in the complicated vortex of the Balkan Peninsula. Regarding the issue of Austrian independence, Germany believes that the Danube Convention is only interesting in reducing Italy's power in Vienna. Regarding the Sky Mutual Assistance Pact, Germany believes that a general solution should be made on the issue of armaments. Germany is willing to join and should enjoy the right to equip a strong air force and possess thousands of military aircraft. As for the issue of returning to the League of Nations, this reply may not mention it in detail, because Germany believes that the content of the League of Nations is not pure and needs to be reorganized. (Twelfth Havas Telegram)

Beijing – The Belgian government has just formally notified the British government, stating its support for the declaration issued by Britain and France in London on February 3 and is willing to participate in the Western European Sky Agreement. (Twelfth Havas Telegram)

Austrian Premier's Visit to England Itinerary

(London) Austrian Prime Minister Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Wiedner will arrive here on the 24th of this month for a visit to England. A banquet will be held that evening by the Duke and Duchess of Londonderry, the Air Minister, to welcome them. The next day at noon, Prime Minister MacDonald will host a banquet to welcome them. On the 26th at noon, Foreign Secretary Simon will host a banquet at the Foreign Ministry. (Eleventh Havas Telegram)

Draft Indian Constitution Approved on Second Reading by British Parliament

Debate Fiercest on Dominion Status

Labor Party Amendment Ultimately Rejected

Baldwin Claims No Intention to Consider General Election

(London) During today's House of Commons debate on the second reading of the government's India Bill, Labor Party members of the opposition put forward an amendment arguing for the explicit acknowledgment of India's right to attain dominion status. After a vote, it was defeated by 404 votes to 133. Lord President of the Council Baldwin, in closing the debate, declared that the government did not wish to consider the question of a general election. There was much to be done now, and he hoped the House would work hard. (The cabinet benches cheered.) He had previously announced a period of thirty days for debating the India Bill, and nervous newspapers were interpreting this announcement of the procedure as a prelude to a general election around Christmas. (Eleventh Reuters dispatch)

(London) A total of 133 opposed the government's India Bill, including 80 Conservative Party members, 48 Labor Party members, 3 Independent Labor Party members, and 2 Independents. That so many Conservatives opposed the bill was quite unexpected. Of the 404 who supported the government, 28 were Liberal Party members, but Liberal Party leader Lloyd George did not vote. (Sixteenth Reuters dispatch)

(London) The government's India Bill has now passed its second reading. During the debate, the question of dominion status was debated most fiercely. Attorney General Inskip declared that, with regard to the dominion status that could be applied to India, the Statute of Westminster granted unlimited legislative power, except in matters affecting the constitution. Although granted equal status, it must remain within the British Empire. There was no question of India having the right to secede from the empire. All of Britain's promises to India were conditional on India not seceding from the empire. Churchill, who had previously been a strong critic of the India Bill, rose to speak, but his tone this time was unexpectedly mild, saying that he and his friends did not want to obstruct the bill. He argued that autonomy should first be granted to the provinces, so that the central government could intervene to prevent the degradation of public works. He made this argument because he deeply felt the need to protect the interests of the people, and that a plan to give power to a small number of people was contrary to democracy. Labor Party leader Lansbury said that the bill had been drafted without genuine consultation with the Indian people, and that he believed the Indian people should draft their own plan, which should include the theoretical right to secede from the empire, as with other dominions. However, he was confident that India would never exercise this right. Lord President of the Council Baldwin said that timely and generous concessions had won India's loyalty to the empire, and that we now offered India an opportunity to take a major step to become a full member of the empire, and that we should offer this opportunity in a spirit of willingness, generosity, and trust. (Eleventh Reuters dispatch)

Young Inventors of Soviet Russia

TASS Moscow, January 5. The All-Union Exhibition of Children's Mechanical Engineering Products is being held here, featuring 2,000 children's inventions. For example, Leningrad's Akiavit, only 15 years old, invented an electric gas stove. Among the young inventors, the Ilyukhin siblings from the Tula region are the most famous. One of the younger brothers, aged 11, has invented an automatic street lamp switch, and his brother, aged 12, has invented an electric dry film machine. Another example is Rameev of Bashkiria, aged 15, who invented a wireless train. There are now 647 children's technical stations throughout the Soviet Union to enhance children's interest in technology. In rural areas, there are also children's agricultural stations, in which many children participate.

Doihara's Activities in Peiping

Reportedly, a Dawn Has Appeared in Sino-Japanese Relations

Will Visit Various Dignitaries in Shanghai and Then in Beijing

(Peiping Communication) Doihara, the director of the Special Service Agency of the Kwantung Army stationed in Shenyang, has entered the pass with open activity. Because the people of the country remember that Pu Yi was taken to Dalian by Doihara alone in the past, they all feel that Doihara's coming here is unfathomable. Doihara lived in Peiping before the Northeast Incident, residing in Chunshu Hutong. During the Beiyang government era, the East Asia Association, jointly formed by Chinese and Japanese nationals, was located at East Single Third Street. The Chinese president was Xiong Xiling, and the Japanese president was Sakatani Rihachiro. When Sakatani returned to his country, Doihara succeeded him as president. Doihara was known as a "China expert." The association was later disbanded due to the dispersal of its members, and Doihara was no longer noticed. After Pu Yi was kidnapped in Tianjin, Doihara became famous and served as the director of the Special Service Agency of the Kwantung Army stationed in Dalian and Shenyang. Although he continued to travel between Peiping and Shenyang, his secret whereabouts attracted the attention of the general public. Recently, Doihara suddenly arrived in Peiping under the pretext of investigation and visiting friends. He visited He Yingqin, Chairman of the Military Sub-Committee, and also visited various agency leaders and old friends in Peiping, engaging in very busy socializing. The reporter visited Doihara at his residence, who readily received him. After the greetings, the reporter first asked about the purpose of this trip. Doihara replied that it was purely a private tour to investigate the local situation. Officials such as Minister He, Yuan Liang, and old friends such as Wang Shulu, Tang Erhe, and Yin Tongsheng had all been met, and he was very happy privately. The reporter then asked about the future itinerary. It was said that the investigation in Peiping was completed, and he would go to Tianjin for a short visit, stay for two days, and then go to Shanghai and then to Beijing by sea. In Shanghai and Beijing, he plans to meet with dignitaries in your country and make ordinary greetings. My trip to various places in China is purely a private activity, and since I do not represent any party to have any contact with the Chinese government, there is no task to speak of. At this point, the reporter smiled and asked if he could tell us about his impressions in Peiping. He replied that he was very satisfied. Later, when the Sino-Japanese relations issue was discussed, Doihara said that, according to his personal feelings, judging from the current situation of the two countries, he believed that a dawn has appeared. If both sides can treat each other with sincerity, the future avenue can naturally benefit both sides. Doihara then talked about the diplomatic commentary on the Sino-Japanese relations review paper written by Xu Daolin, and said that this article is indeed a public opinion in the Sino-Japanese problem, and it is no different from opening a viable path to solve the Sino-Japanese problem. On the Japanese side, it has aroused deep interest. In your country, it can be called a kind of courageous public opinion. I personally admire it very much. However, how to put this problem into practice depends on the joint research of politicians and intellectuals in both countries in order to seek a simple way to achieve twice the result with half the effort and share the success. If so, it will be of no small benefit to the friendship between China and Japan. At this point, because there were visitors, the reporter said goodbye and left. Doihara hosted a banquet at the Hotel des Nations today (the 9th) at noon to answer all parties, and then left Peiping for Tianjin at 4:30 p.m. It was scheduled to take a ship from Tianjin to Shanghai the day after tomorrow (the 11th). It is said that Doihara will stay in Shanghai for four days, and then go to Beijing. According to reliable sources, although Doihara has repeatedly stated that he has not shouldered any task for this entry, his task is implicit in what he said about the investigation. Doihara is between the steady and young factions in the Japanese Kwantung Army. His words and deeds may influence the general thinking of soldiers. Therefore, Doihara's future words and deeds after returning to Shenyang are also worthy of attention. (9th)

Gansu Province Financial Reorganization Situation

Abolish the Appropriation System

Abolish Unjust Taxes

(Lanzhou Communication) Gansu is located in a remote border area and has always been known as a poor area. During the Qing Dynasty, it was a province that received subsidies. After the establishment of the Republic of China, the subsidies were cut off, and military expenses greatly increased, resulting in a deficit of about 4 million yuan. The provincial treasury owed more than 10 million yuan, and the person in charge of finance was unable to cope. Therefore, the appropriation system became the only means of turnover, allowing the requisitioning agencies to extract from the collecting agencies. The amount of appropriations often exceeded the additional requisitions from various counties and bureaus. Once an appropriation was ordered, it had to be apportioned to the people, burdening officials and harming the people. The abuses were endless. Director of the Department of Finance Zhu Jingzhou, upon taking office last year, keenly understood the abuses and urgently considered eliminating them. Due to the Ningxia War, discussions were repeatedly interrupted and failed to be implemented. Now, Mr. Zhu has carefully planned the military and political expenses in detail, and has presented them to the provincial government for approval last year. From January of this year, the appropriation system will be abolished in the following counties of Longdong: Pingliang, Jingning, Longde, Zhuanglang, Huaping, Guyuan, Haiyuan, Qingyang, Ningxian, Heshui, Zhenning, Huanxian, Jingchuan, Chongxin, Zhenyuan, Lingtai, Huating, etc.; the following counties of Longnan: Tianshui, Xihe, Gangu, Wushan, Qin'an, Qingshui, Lixian, Huixian, Chengxian, Liangdang, Wudu, Wenxian, Xigu, Kangxian, etc.; and the following counties in the old Lanshan Road District: Gaolan, Linxia, Lintao, Hezheng, Yongjing, Xiahe, Ningding, Jingyuan, Longxi, Tongwei, Zhangxian, Yuzhong, Taosha, Weiyuan, Dingxi, Jingqin, Lintan, Minxian, Huining, etc. The appropriation system will be abolished first to alleviate the people's difficulties. The counties in Hexi are currently being planned in a comprehensive manner. It is expected that by the end of this year, the appropriations in the entire province can be completely cancelled. In addition, since the central government abolished the Likin tax in 1931, it has repeatedly ordered various provinces to abolish unjust taxes. Gansu, due to its special circumstances and financial difficulties, has not been able to implement this. It is now heard that Director Zhu of the Department of Finance, in accordance with the central government's intention to relieve the people's suffering, has decided to abolish the taxes in stages. Fifty-seven types of taxes that are overly burdensome and detrimental to the livelihood of civilians, totaling more than 380,000 yuan per year, have been listed and reported as the first phase, to be abolished first from January 1, 1935. Personnel have also been dispatched to various districts to investigate, and they will be abolished gradually after a detailed report. A list of abolished unjust taxes is attached below:

(1) Under the Category of Additional Taxes

Tax Category Annual Revenue Additional Tax on Special Consumption Tax 10% Stamp Tax 116,000 yuan Additional Tax on Livestock Tax 10% Stamp Tax 20,000 yuan Additional Tax on Slaughter Tax 10% Stamp Tax 2,500 yuan Additional Tax on Cigarette Inspection Tax 10% Stamp Tax 10,000 yuan Additional Tax on Camel Tax 10% Stamp Tax 7,500 yuan Additional Tax on Tobacco and Alcohol Tax 10% Stamp Tax 50,200 yuan Additional Tax on Opium Suppression Surtax 10% Stamp Tax 60,100 yuan Additional Tax on Salt Tax 10% Stamp Tax 60,000 yuan

(2) Under the Category of Additional Taxes on Land Tax

Tax Category Annual Revenue

Curriculum 3,633.50 yuan Land Tax 511 yuan Tribute 353 yuan Medicinal Herbs 866 yuan

Madder 775.40 yuan Shop Padding 3,588.50 yuan Annual Example 139.20 yuan Foot Price 599.70 yuan Artisan Price 346.55 yuan Bonus 357.60 yuan Garrison Rent 259.40 yuan Ding Station 68.57 yuan Agriculture and Sericulture 17.53 yuan

(3) Under the Category of Special Taxes

Goods Name Annual Revenue

Local Porcelain 6,000.00 yuan 1.20 fen Black Porcelain 5,001.58 yuan Persimmons 500 yuan Red Soil 200.05 yuan Glutinous Rice Flour 310 yuan Pomegranates 300 yuan Dried Cabbage 200 yuan Wood Pear 400.02 yuan Corn Sugar 302.50 yuan Fresh Pork 1,000.35 yuan Cooked Pork 213 yuan Felt Clothing 3,003.30 yuan Coarse Red and White Felt 5,000 yuan Wool Pockets 1,003.70 yuan Fine Red and White Felt 2,005.05 yuan Coarse Felt Hats 1,000 yuan Coarse Cloth 1,004.50 yuan Velvet Bibs 510 yuan Cloth Bibs 301.10 yuan Cloth Quilt Covers 500 yuan Cloth Mattress Covers 401.20 yuan Cloth Money Bags 300 yuan Tangerines and Oranges 507 yuan Water Chestnuts 203 yuan Various Surveying Instruments 2,000 yuan Various Chemical Testing Instruments 1,500.07 yuan Various Drawing Instruments 2,000 yuan Beef Tallow Candles 1,500 yuan Mutton Tallow Candles 1,000 yuan Yams 800.30 yuan Noodle Paste 509.30 yuan Soy Sauce 506 yuan Soy Bean Sprouts 700 yuan Hairy Taro 212 yuan Persimmon Cakes 602 yuan Fresh Lilies The total for the above 57 items is 383,313.75 yuan per year.

Songjiang

Robbed While Going to the Toilet at Night

Yang Xiangjin, the younger brother of farmer Yang Hesheng in Shantou Temple, was attacked while going to the toilet in the back of his house around midnight the night before. Notorious bandit Wu Suisheng (aka Xiao Asan) ambushed him outside the door, pushed Yang Xiangjin down, and stabbed him with a sharp blade. Yang shouted for help, and his brother heard the noise and called for help. Neighbor Chu Axiang came out to help capture the bandit. They immediately reported to Qin Shihai, the first squad leader of the first company of the twelfth security brigade, who led his team to the scene and arrested the criminal Wu Suisheng at the squad headquarters. During interrogation, Wu confessed to stabbing Yang and also confessed to robbing a family named Mou in the north of Hougang of four and a half piculs of white rice and cloth while selling smuggled salt on the thirteenth day of the eighth lunar month last year. On the night of the ninth day of the lunar month, he robbed a family in a thatched house on Xin Street of white rice and clothing. He confessed that he had five accomplices and that he had mortgaged a Mauser rifle at the Zhou family in the west of Changshan Dam, Haiyan, Zhejiang, for 16 yuan. Captain Qin has escorted the bandit to the brigade headquarters yesterday to await verification and handling.

Suzhou

New Trend in Various Industries Requesting Reduced Electricity Rates

Various associations in Suzhou, such as the Iron and Machinery Industry Association and the Silk Weaving Industry Association, have repeatedly petitioned various departments and provinces, requesting that the Suzhou Electric Plant reduce the electricity rates for motors. The details of this process have been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. It is now known that local figures have been appointed to mediate. After the chairman of the Iron and Machinery Industry Association, Liu Fuqing, and the manager of the Electric Plant, Ding Chunzhi, contacted each other on the 12th, a peaceful solution is expected. In addition, the Construction Bureau and some electricity users believe that the street light lines used by the plant are old lines from 15 years ago, and there is no outer covering on the lines. Eight years ago, there was a tragic accident in which firefighter Shi Jinkui was electrocuted to death. So many years have passed, and they have not been replaced, which is very dangerous. They are currently negotiating with the electric plant authorities, requesting that the new cable be replaced to avoid danger. If this goal cannot be achieved, it is feared that disputes will arise again.

Wuxi

The Fifth Public Security Bureau Subverted

Yesterday morning after one o'clock, the Wuxi County Public Security Bureau received a report that gambling activities were taking place in the Wang residence in Bu Xiang Alley outside the North Gate. The Inspectorate dispatched over fifty officers and police to arrest those involved. Upon arriving at the Wang residence, it was discovered that the location was the dormitory of the First Aid Society's fire brigade of the First District and the defense post of the Ninth Detachment of the merchant corps. It being fire prevention season, most of the brigade members were already asleep. The police officers searched the premises but found nothing, and there was no sign of gambling. Upon questioning by the brigade members, the police officers successively withdrew. However, after the search, the interior was left in disarray, and the door lamp was broken. Suddenly, alarm gongs sounded, reporting a fire at the Fifth Public Security Bureau in Jiangyin Alley. The fire brigades of various sections, not knowing the truth, rushed out of their warm beds to drag their water pumps to the rescue. Some even went to the Dahe Pond behind the bureau to draw water for firefighting. At that time, the bureau chief, Hong Houchang, and bureau staff member Gu Songxun were out on patrol. The police officers inside the bureau and nearby sentry police also fled, leaving only the gate sentry, Wei Lanting, who urgently declared to the fire brigades that there was no fire. However, the crowd was large and chaotic, and the interior items, doors, windows, desks, and tables were all damaged. Fortunately, no firearms were missing. Although the prisoners in the detention center were soaked with water, none escaped. At that time, the county government, the Public Security Bureau, and the Joint Fire Brigade had received reports. Xu Yi, the detachment commander of the security team, and Feng Ziqian, the captain of the third company, immediately led their teams to the scene to suppress the situation. The Joint Fire Brigade also sent personnel. Only then did the firefighters and bystanders disperse in confusion. All the fire engines and water hoses from various sections' fire brigades, totaling twelve units, were placed in front of the Fifth Public Security Bureau. Afterward, the bureau chief Hong and staff member Gu successively reported to the Public Security Bureau, who then reported to County Magistrate Yan, awaiting resolution. The person who reported the gambling was temporarily detained at the Public Security Bureau, awaiting further investigation.

Yangzhou

The Zhen Tai Steamer Collides with Bridge and Capsizes

The Zhen Tai steamer of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, while sailing from Zhenjiang to Nantong on the tenth morning, was passing by a large bridge near Yiling Town. As usual at 8 PM, it was required to wait for the bridge to be raised before passing through. Unexpectedly, the steamer was traveling too fast and the current was strong, causing the steamer to collide with the bridge pier and capsize. Dozens of passengers fell into the water at that time. Although nearby boats provided rescue, it was nighttime, and the exact number of passengers who drowned was difficult to ascertain.

To Inspect Customs Administration in Europe and America

Wo Modu Also on the Same Ship Returning to Italy

He boarded the Italian ship Conte Verde at ten o'clock last night to go to Italy.

(A recent photo of Mr. Ding Guitang)

The ship raised anchor at five o'clock this morning and is expected to arrive in Italy on March 9. Mr. Ding is from Liaoning and graduated from the Beijing Customs College. He is well-versed in customs research and is also very capable in handling affairs. Therefore, he was promoted to Tax Inspector of the General Affairs Department of the Inspectorate General of Customs. According to Mr. Ding, he plans to go to Italy first and then to Germany, France, England, the United States, and other countries to inspect the customs administration of these advanced countries, so that he can make recommendations to the Ministry of Finance for adoption and implementation after returning to China. The trip is scheduled for six months, and he is expected to return to China between August and September of this year. Mr. Ding has been busy with banquets given by customs colleagues and relatives in recent days. When he boarded the ship at ten o'clock yesterday afternoon, Tang Haian, the Customs Superintendent, Bode, the Commissioner of the Jianghai Customs, and the staff of various departments of the Inspectorate General of Customs, as well as relatives and friends of Mr. Ding, all went to see him off. Furthermore, the Italian water conservancy expert Wo Modu, who was sent to China last year to inspect water conservancy in various places, has now completed his work. Therefore, he boarded the Italian mail ship Conte Verde with Mr. Ding at approximately ten o'clock last night and set sail at four o'clock this morning to return to Italy, where he will report to the League of Nations in Geneva.

Civil Servants Wearing Domestic Goods Clothing

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce Instructs the International Trade Bureau

The Shanghai International Trade Bureau received Instruction No. 11552 of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, which stated: "According to Instruction No. 42 of the Executive Yuan dated January 5, 1935, and Letter No. 967 of the National Government, the fifth plenary session of the fourth session of this council approved the motion submitted by Wu Jingheng and four other members to request the government to take practical measures to relieve the panic of yarn mills throughout the country, promote the sale of native cloth to benefit the people's livelihood and maintain enterprises." The following resolutions were adopted: "(1) The government should contact the financial sector to promote mutual support with the national yarn industry and implement low-interest loans to alleviate the lack of capital. (2) Within the possible scope, appropriately increase import tariffs and reduce domestic taxes. (3) The government should implement organized production and sales through controls. (4) The location of national yarn mills must be appropriately allocated, and management and production must be scientific and rationalized. (5) All national civil servants, party workers, school teachers, and students must wear domestic goods and absolutely prohibit wearing non-domestic goods clothing." Except for item 5, which has been ordered to all levels of the party headquarters for compliance, the corresponding letter is hereby communicated for investigation, reference, and distribution to the competent authorities for handling (the following omitted).

The Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee Temporarily Suspends the Purchase of Silver for Shipment to Shanghai for Regulation

The Three Banks Extended the Loan Repayment Period After Closing Accounts

The Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee has decided to temporarily suspend the purchase of Hong Kong silver for shipment to Shanghai for regulation due to a shortage of silver in Hong Kong. The details are as follows:

The Stabilization Committee Temporarily Suspends the Purchase of Hong Kong Silver: In order to stabilize the market, the Foreign Exchange Stabilization Committee entrusted the Hong Kong branches of the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications to purchase silver for shipment to Shanghai for regulation. The first, second, third, fourth, and fifth batches arrived in Shanghai before the end of 1934, totaling 2,312,000 yuan in national currency. The original total purchase amount was 20 million yuan. As the closing account period for various industries in Shanghai has passed, the purchase has been temporarily suspended. A decision will be made in the future based on future needs. As for the sixth batch of cash, it is rumored that it has already been loaded on the Great American Company's Coolidge for shipment to Shanghai. The reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency visited the three committee members of the committee yesterday morning, and they all stated that they had not heard of it.

The Three Banks Released Loans to Regulate Finance: In view of the urgent silver shortage in Shanghai, the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, in order to regulate finance, held a large amount of cash to provide to silver and money businesses. Before the end of 1934, up to the closing account day of February 3, a total of more than 8 million yuan was released. Now, most of these loans have been extended for repayment, except for a small number that have been recovered. No new loans have been released after the closing of accounts, but it has been decided to continue handling mortgage loans at any time, depending on the needs of the market.

After the end of 1934, various industries have opened one after another. The daily published foreign exchange interest rates in the money market, except for two points on the first day, have been six points for several consecutive days. It is found that every time after the end of the closing of accounts, when money shops enter the market, because the demand for cash among money shop colleagues is relatively small, the foreign exchange interest rate is usually a white premium.

Stayed in Japan and Taiwan for two months and thoroughly investigated the planting of tea trees and the method of tea production. Japan currently produces a total of 5 million dan of tea, and Taiwan approximately 2 million dan. Although the quantity is not large, when compared with China, it is only equivalent to China's export quantity. However, the quantity that increases each year is extremely alarming. There is still a trend of increasing year by year, and their attention to the equipment of tea is far better than that of China. For example, Japan spent more than 3 million yuan on tea equipment last year. As a result, its quality is also becoming increasingly superior, and both quality and quantity have been improved. China's tea industry is sticking to old methods and not making any improvements. As a result, the international sales market is gradually declining, and Japanese tea has the potential to encroach on Chinese tea. If improvements are not made quickly, the future is truly unimaginable. I also plan to go to Nanyang for further inspection and will set off within a few days. After returning from Nanyang, I will draft a report and submit it to the National Economic Council for reference as a basis for improving China's tea industry.

The Central Bank Announces the Collection and Exchange of Assorted Silver Materials

Starting in Shanghai on the 25th

Simplified Rules Promulgated with the Approval of the Ministry of Finance

The Central Bank, upon the order of the Ministry of Finance, has established a Collection and Exchange Office for Assorted Silver Materials, which is managed by the Cashier Section of the Business Bureau. An announcement was made yesterday, stating that collection and exchange will begin in Shanghai on February 25th. The details are as follows:

Announcement from the Central Bank: According to the Ministry of Finance's letter, the Shanghai Money Trade Association has reported that silver ornaments and silver ingots owned by the people have no sales channels since the silver furnaces were ordered to close. It is proposed that the Central Bank be requested to collect and exchange them and send them to the mint to recast them into national currency for turnover. Accordingly, this bank and its branches shall set up collection and exchange offices for assorted silver materials for collection and exchange. After a certain amount has been collected, they shall be sent to the Central Mint for melting and casting into national currency. This bank shall act accordingly. This bank has decided to start collection and exchange in Shanghai on February 25th. Those who hold the above-mentioned assorted silver materials are requested to come to the bank to obtain the simplified rules for the collection and exchange of assorted silver materials, fill out the application form, and exchange them for national currency. The date of collection and exchange in other places will be announced later. The Central Bank hereby announces. Simplified Rules: Simplified Rules for the Central Bank's Collection and Exchange of Assorted Silver Materials. (1) This bank is entrusted by the Ministry of Finance to collect and exchange assorted silver materials for the convenience of merchants and people. Those who hold the above-mentioned silver materials may deliver them to this bank for collection and exchange at any time. (2) Assorted silver materials weighing more than 1,500 grams are not subject to the provisions of the preceding article and shall be handled in accordance with the regulations of this bank for managing the minting of silver coins. (Regulations for managing the minting of silver coins are as follows: Those who entrust casting must notify the bank in writing in advance of the amount of silver, and the bank will specify the date and jointly send it to the Central Mint for collection and casting. The bank will temporarily issue a temporary receipt. Once the mint has completed the melting and casting, they can collect the silver standard currency according to the number on the minting list of the mint.) (3) When delivering assorted silver materials to this bank for collection and exchange, a main and a copy of the application form must be filled out. The weight and reason number of the silver material in the application form must be filled in after verification by this bank. (The application form can be obtained from this bank.) (4) The weight of the assorted silver materials shall be based on the standard system. (5) After this bank estimates the fineness and weight of the assorted silver materials, it will calculate them in accordance with the regulations of the silver standard coin minting regulations, with each yuan equivalent to 23.493448 grams of pure silver, and deduct the casting fee and melting chain according to law. In places other than Shanghai, this bank shall also pay the agent exchange fee (including advance interest, transportation insurance, handling fees, etc.). The fee shall be calculated by this bank at any time. (6) This bank may refuse to collect and exchange assorted silver materials for which it has doubts. (7) Assorted silver materials that have been exchanged may not be applied for recovery or objection afterward. (8) The exchange time is from 10:00 AM to 12:00 PM and 2:00 PM to 3:00 PM every day except holidays, and until 12:00 PM on Saturdays. (9) These simplified rules shall be implemented after being approved by the Ministry of Finance, and the same shall apply to amendments.

The Shanghai Yarn and Cloth, Securities, Gold, Flour, and Miscellaneous Grains stock exchange brokers' associations, feeling unable to bear the burden of the Ministry of Finance's scheduled collection of transaction taxes, held their ninth joint meeting at the Yarn and Cloth Stock Exchange Brokers' Association yesterday at 4:00 PM.
