Attending Representatives: Yesterday's attendees included Bian Futang, Kuang Jian, Zhang Bojin, and Shao Wenmei from the Yarn and Cloth Stock Exchange; Wang Yingchang, Wang Jiafu, and Zhan Liansheng from the Gold Stock Exchange; Wang Zhengru and Wu Limen from the Securities Stock Exchange; Zhang Weiyun, Zhu Jiansheng, Yang Jingcheng, and Wang Zhongliang from the Flour Stock Exchange; and Xue Chengzhang from the Miscellaneous Grains Stock Exchange, totaling over a dozen people.

Resolutions: Bian Futang was elected chairman. After formal greetings, the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting and then began discussion. 1) Regarding the Ministry of Finance's collection of transaction taxes, although the Legislative Yuan has reduced various tax rates, it is difficult to bear this burden during this time of commercial depression. How should this Association express its views? It was resolved: (A) Telegraph the Central Government requesting a delay; (B) Send a letter to the Federation of Stock Exchanges to take unified action; (C) Recent newspaper reports have stated that some people advocate requesting the government to postpone collection for one year. This news is inaccurate and a letter should be sent to the Federation of Stock Exchanges to correct the reports. The meeting adjourned at approximately 7:00 PM. According to a reporter from the Industrial and Commercial News Agency, if the association's request is not granted by the Ministry of Finance, it is determined to send representatives to petition in Beijing again, not stopping until the objective is achieved.

Telegraph Requesting a Delay in Collection: Yesterday, the association telegraphed the Central Political Council, National Government Chairman Lin, Military Affairs Commission Chairman Chiang, Legislative Yuan President Sun, Executive Yuan President Wang, Minister of Finance Kong, and Minister of Industry Chen, stating: "We have recently seen reports that the Legislative Yuan has reduced the tax rates of the transaction tax regulations for stock exchanges, showing your esteemed Yuan and Ministry's deep understanding of the hardships faced by businesses. Associations like ours dare not be silent. Due to the pressing circumstances, we venture to telegraph again, hoping for your kind consideration. We have previously reported that an economic crisis is imminent, and we have repeatedly appealed regarding the difficult circumstances of businesses. We did not expect that within a month, various flaws would emerge rapidly and the level of panic would worsen day by day. During the accounting period in Shanghai's financial circles, due to fluctuations in the overall economic malaise, various loans could not be recovered upon maturity, leading to difficulties and illiquidity. The situation is precarious and fraught with danger. As a result, nearly ten Huihua Qianzhuang (money shops) which are members of the Shanghai Qianye Dagonghui, known for their sound organization and strong financial resources, have been liquidated and closed, accounting for a strong tenth of the total membership of the industry. Other industries, factories, and shops have closed or suspended business one after another, facing precarious situations. The urgency of the situation is becoming increasingly apparent. Although various industries have resumed business as usual after the Spring Festival holiday, they have all fallen into a lifeless state due to financial exhaustion. Regarding the daily turnover of associations like ours, new transactions have been very few since the beginning of spring, presenting a bleak picture unseen in recent years. The rapid and widespread spread of the economic downturn is even more severe than when associations like ours previously reported. We observe that the serious prelude to future disasters is just beginning. The financial crisis is such, and the commercial recession is such. Merchants are in difficult times, and if they want to maintain the status quo, they are still worried about various problems. How can they bear to pay taxes? Although the collection of this tax was previously stipulated by your esteemed Yuan and Ministry, in this extraordinary period of commercial depression, the burden on businesses will inevitably increase, and transactions will inevitably decrease. The impact is unimaginable. Associations like ours have repeatedly considered that we can only request your esteemed Yuan and Ministry to consider the current difficulties and allow the tax case to be postponed. Under these circumstances, it is by no means possible to bear it within three to five years, and we should wait for the market to recover to a prosperous and normal state before collecting it, so that both national taxes and commercial strength can be considered, and we can uphold the late Premier's legacy of the Principle of People's Livelihood, and show the government's intention to let the people rest. The future of commerce really depends on this. In addition, public bonds and treasury bills are issued by the state, and there is no precedent for taxation in countries around the world. If they are taxed in the same way as other marketable securities, it is tantamount to restricting people's investment in national debt. In terms of both reason and sentiment, it should be inappropriate. We request the Legislative Yuan to remove public bonds and treasury bills from the category of marketable securities and exempt them from taxation with explicit provisions. The above requests are humbly submitted for approval and implementation, which would be a great kindness. We are extremely fearful and await orders. Respectfully presented by Bian Futang, representative of the Shanghai Chinese Yarn and Cloth Stock Exchange Brokers' Association; Wang Zhengru, representative of the Securities Stock Exchange Brokers' Association; Zhan Liansheng, representative of the Gold Stock Exchange Brokers' Association; Zhang Janyun, representative of the Flour Stock Exchange Brokers' Association; and Xue Chengzhang, representative of the Miscellaneous Grains Stock Exchange Brokers' Association."

Public Bond Transactions are Legitimate and Legal Business

Futures Trading of Public Bonds Cannot Be Considered Speculation

According to Xin Xin News Agency, it was reported on the 8th of this month that during the discussion of the transaction tax in the Legislative Yuan, it was stated that the futures trading of public bonds has a speculative nature. A reporter from Xin Xin News Agency met Mr. Zhang Weiru from the financial sector yesterday to discuss this matter. Mr. Zhang said, "Public bond transactions are originally legitimate and legal business. The occurrence of buying and selling depends entirely on the needs of supply and demand, with prices determined accordingly. Sometimes, when financing is tight, the bond price is low and supply exceeds demand. When financing is relaxed, the bond interest rate is low and demand is high. For example, individuals or shops may have payments due and estimate the time required to purchase futures, earning interest on a regular basis. Conversely, they may sell futures to cope with payments. Through cycles of buying and selling, the futures market becomes prosperous." He further elaborated: "(A) Financial institutions or individuals purchase bonds for the current month and sell futures for the next month, calculating the difference between principal and interest to earn profits. This is called arbitrage in commercial terms. The turnaround is convenient, and the term is not long. The amount of interest depends on the tightness of financing. Since there are accurate estimates, the business is not risky. It is purely an investment and definitely not speculation. (B) Investors in bonds are not limited to Shanghai. The securities market is centered in Shanghai, so merchants from other places entrust securities brokers to buy and sell through letters and telegrams. Even if there is spot trading, it is difficult to transport the goods in advance. Therefore, futures trading must be done to prepare for delivery upon maturity. (C) Shops or individuals plan to invest in public bonds, but the current cash is expected to be received in a certain period of time. Therefore, they purchase futures for the next month and receive the goods upon maturity." The above three points cannot be solved by spot trading alone. Judging from the situation in Shanghai, the first two types account for the majority of transactions. The market is becoming increasingly busy because of this. The financial sector uses this to circulate funds, adjust surpluses and deficits, and popularize it among the masses. The credit of public bonds is becoming increasingly solid, and national economy and social finance rely on it. It seems a bit theoretical to call it speculation. In fact, these types of transactions can definitely not be considered speculation."

The Two Railways Issue Notices to Pay Attention to On-Time Train Operation

Shanghai-Ping Train Arrives More Than Half an Hour Late

Should Make the Greatest Determination to Maintain and Improve

The Vehicle Affairs and Locomotive Affairs Departments of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus jointly issued Notice No. 81 the day before yesterday, stating: "On-time train operation is the most important goal of the railway. Although the traffic density of railways in Europe and the United States is high, passenger trains rarely arrive late. On the other hand, the Shanghai-Ping train often arrives more than half an hour late. Fast trains and express trains often arrive about two hours late. In addition, it is rare for regional trains and slow trains to arrive on time. The reasons for the delays are extremely complex, but the employees of our Vehicle Affairs and Locomotive Affairs Departments are most closely related. Self-improvement is essential for rectification. In the future, all relevant employees of the Vehicle Affairs and Locomotive Affairs Departments should make the greatest determination to maintain and improve on-time train operation. Even a minute's delay should be avoided. If a train is delayed, regardless of whether the reason belongs to the Vehicle Affairs, Locomotive Affairs, or other aspects, the employees of the Vehicle Affairs and Locomotive Affairs Departments should regard it as a major issue and a disgrace. They must report the details truthfully for verification and handling. If there are suggestions for improvement regarding equipment, personnel, or employee perceptions, they should be reported in detail for our departments to take remedial measures. Those who do well will be rewarded, and those who are perfunctory or mismanaged will be severely punished upon verification. Our departments have made the greatest determination. All relevant employees must understand our departments' intention to rectify train operation, encourage each other, and not regard it as a mere formality, lest they be found guilty of serious violations. This notice is issued jointly for strict compliance."

Moreover, its location at Xianxia, with overlapping mountains and sparse fields, means that even in years of good harvests, it is only self-sufficient. Those who dug ferns and boiled grass to satisfy their hunger and those who sold their sons and daughters blocked the roads. The tragic deaths were scattered everywhere, and the fleeing refugees were unbearable to hear or see. Although the dangerous city was finally secured and the fierce bandits were driven back, the essence of the local area was almost completely lost. Jiangshan, with its poor people and exhausted wealth, suffered these two major disasters. The dead cannot be brought back to life, and the scars are everywhere. Without considerable relief, the people will inevitably become bandits. Moreover, there are still many bandits on the border who will come out at any opportunity. Without a way to eliminate them, how can we prevent them from recurring? We dare to ask for the allocation of benevolent syrup to save our disaster victims. The 3,000 members of the church and 310,000 people of Jiangshan are waiting with great anticipation to thank you, etc. After reading this report, with the commerce in Shanghai so depressed and the disasters in various places so serious, people with compassion are at a loss and can only cry together.

China Travel Service Establishes Inns in Beishan and Wuxie

Zhuji Wuxie and Jinhua Beishan on the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway are famous scenic spots in eastern Zhejiang. Recently, with the beautiful spring and pleasant scenery, people from all over the world have been visiting in droves. In order to entertain tourists from afar, the China Travel Service has specially sent personnel to plan to establish inns in suitable locations in the two famous scenic spots to provide food and lodging for tourists. In addition, the fees for baggage handling and river crossing at each station along the railway have always been quoted in foreign currencies. As the market prices in various places fluctuate, it is inevitable that there will be trickery and deception of merchants. In view of this, the railway has changed all the above fees to copper coins and made the price list into signs to be hung at each station so that passengers can easily see them.

Annual Business Report of the Electric Power Company

Surplus of Over Six Million

The Shanghai Electric Power Company has released its business report for the year ending December 31, 1934. The surplus for the year is 6,033,962.47 yuan, and the public reserve is 6,136,360.53 yuan. The company's total maintenance cost for the year was approximately 1,423,000 yuan, and the cost for improvement and expansion was 2,842,332.82 yuan. The new 22,500 kilowatt unit installed in the Jiangbin Power Plant in the spring of 1933 was completed in August last year. This is the largest item in the project. In addition, several new lines have been added for industrial use, and a new 6,000 kilowatt transmission unit has been added to the Chaoyang Road branch.

Silk and Satin Prices Expected to Rise This Year

Interview with Wu Zhihao, Leader of the Silk and Satin Industry

Price Increase is Not Surprising

Prices May be Higher After Autumn

Since the resumption of business after the Spring Festival holiday, the prices of various goods in the Shanghai silk and satin industry have increased slightly. At this time of economic downturn, this price increase has surprised many people in society. A reporter from Guowen News Agency met with Wu Zhihao, a leader in the silk and satin industry, yesterday. According to him, the price increase in the silk and satin industry is not surprising. Every year after the opening of business after the New Year, prices will increase slightly, and then gradually decrease after the new spring silkworm cocoons enter the market. This year is the same. The main reason is that inventories are not high, and the demand in the market has not decreased. However, there are special circumstances this year, that is, in the past few decades, after the New Year, each store had to purchase a certain amount of goods. However, this year, only a few stores can purchase goods. And according to my observation (Wu said himself), the price of silk will definitely rise after the autumn this year. The main reason is that in recent years, due to the low price of silk, high labor and food costs, silkworm farmers have suffered excessive losses. Raising something else would be better, so it is expected that this year's rearing will be limited.

Huang Jiemin Arrested for Illegally Establishing a Drug Eradication Society

Established Articles of Association and Collected Substantial Fees

Organized and Paraded Without Approval

Huang Jiemin from Suzhou, who previously worked as a clerk for the late lawyer Cai Nipei, saw that Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, had promulgated strict regulations prohibiting potent drugs, and that the central government was also strictly enforcing the ban on opium, aiming to eradicate it nationwide within six years. He then saw a great opportunity to make money and established the "China Public Drug Eradication Society." He rented house number 8, Sanrui Lane, 201 Tongfu Road in western Shanghai as the society's general office. He printed articles of association, declarations, and provisional rules for subsidizing the society's expenses, and distributed them everywhere to recruit members. The qualifications for becoming a member were divided into five categories: (A) Group member, required to contribute 100 yuan annually; (B) Branch member, first-class branch members required to contribute 1,000 yuan annually, second-class 500 yuan, third-class 200 yuan, fourth-class 100 yuan; (C) Basic member, divided into individual and student categories, individuals required to contribute 10 yuan or more annually, students were exempt from fees; (D) Honorary member, required to contribute 100 yuan or more annually; (E) Fee-paying items, stipulating that branch certificates cost 5 yuan each, member badges 2 yuan each, and student badges 1 yuan each. It was also stipulated that those who joined the society, once identified as a certain type of member, should pay all the required fees at once, and failure to pay by the deadline would result in the revocation of membership. The treatment of members was also stipulated. Those who organized branches in various provinces, cities, counties, and districts would have their fees temporarily deferred, and the member certificates and badges they obtained on behalf of the members would be calculated at 75% of the price, with the remaining 25% being the branch's remuneration. If a member could gather three or more like-minded people to join the society, the member's certificate fee would be waived. If more than three people were introduced, 25% of the certificate fee would be offered as a reward. Official members who worked for more than one year and had excellent drug eradication achievements would be recommended by the society to the authorities to be appointed as members of the county opium prohibition committee. Those with special merits would be recommended to the National Government for generous rewards. Huang even submitted the process of organizing the society to the Ministry of Interior of the National Government, the Central Party Headquarters, the Public Guidance Committee, and the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters, hoping to fraudulently register it, in the hope of using government offices as a protective talisman. Internal instructions were successively sent to the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters for submission, but the Municipal Party Headquarters had long been aware of its intentions, and only because it used the name of persuading people to quit opium did not directly denounce it, but only approved that the nature of the society was the same as that of the Drug Resistance Association. Since there was a Drug Resistance Association first, there was no need to establish another name, and they could join the association to work, etc. However, Huang still did not realize it, and repeatedly petitioned the Jiangsu Provincial Government and other agencies, but was rejected. At that time, the Public Concession Bureau of the Shanghai Municipal Council also felt that Huang's actions might hinder the work of the bureau's drug prohibition team, and were suspected of violating Article 165 of the Criminal Law. The bureau's legal team put forward a discussion on whether to ban it. As a result, because no evidence of fraud was found, a laissez-faire attitude was adopted and no interference was made for the time being. Seeing that the police station under its jurisdiction had not interfered, Huang did not regard the approval or disapproval of registration as a measure of progress, and became even more flamboyant. Recently, it was heard by the Nanchang Headquarters of the Military Affairs Commission, which ordered the Shanghai Garrison Command to instruct the Municipal Public Security Bureau to send inspectors Ding Xubao and Wu Yihong to go to the address with Chinese and foreign detectives from the Chengdu Road Police Station the day before yesterday, arrest Huang Jiemin, and search out two wooden seals, 18 badges, five account books, eight official letters, as well as the society's articles of association, declarations, leaflets, and correspondence between members, and bring them all to the police station. He was escorted to the First Special District Local Court yesterday morning, where Judge Wu Tingqi conducted a preliminary hearing. Zhang Tianyin, the police station's lawyer, stated the process of the police station's assistance in arresting Huang and the reasons why the society was not banned immediately when it was established. Next, Zhan Jifeng, the legal advisor of the Public Security Bureau, stated that the society was an illegal organization, and Huang had also interfered with the police power of the Public Security Bureau. Now that he had been arrested by the order of the Nanchang Headquarters of the Military Affairs Commission, he should request permission to transfer him. Judge Wu then questioned Huang Jiemin's confession about the procedures for organizing the society, but firmly denied that he had committed fraud. Finally, Huang's lawyers Fan Gang and Fan Qisheng defended him. As a result, Judge Wu ruled that Huang Jiemin was obviously suspected of fraud and approved the transfer to the representative of the Public Security Bureau, together with the evidence, for investigation. The police station's lawyer requested that Huang be temporarily detained at the police station during the appeal period, which was approved by the court.

The number of silkworms will inevitably decrease, and the price of silk will also inevitably increase, so the price of silk fabrics will also inevitably rise along with the price of silk.

International Trade Bureau Introduces Domestically Produced Goods

Pig Bristles and Flashlight Shells

Pig bristles are the hairs that grow on the back of pigs, as hard as needles, and about two to seven inches long. Their quality is judged by the place of origin, the slaughter period, the length, and the color. Generally, those produced in cold regions are better than those produced in temperate regions. The bristles obtained from the spring slaughter period are better than those obtained from the autumn slaughter period. Long and white bristles are more expensive than short and black ones. Wild boar bristles are more expensive than domestic pig bristles. Their main use is as raw materials for making brushes. White pig bristles can be used for toothbrushes, hairbrushes, and hat brushes. They are often exported from Mongolia, the three northeastern provinces, North China, and Central China to countries such as Britain, France, and the United States, in very large quantities, with Tianjin, Chongqing, and Hankou being the distribution centers. Those produced in Sichuan are of the best quality and occupy an important position in the European market. The Finnish Boromeisen Company needs pig bristles that are five to ten inches long and hopes that exporting merchants will inform the bureau so that it can introduce them.

There are many places in the interior of our country without electric lights, so the demand for flashlights is very high. Therefore, operators of flashlights set up factories to manufacture them, because the capital is small and it is easy to do. There are now many factories in Shanghai that manufacture small light bulbs for flashlights, and there are also many factories that manufacture flashlight shells. Their products are excellent and sell well. The New York Gas Company needs flashlight shells from our country and has specifically sent a letter to the bureau to introduce them. Those who are willing to export this kind of goods can write to the International Trade Bureau for introduction. The address is under the New Rubbish Bridge.

Tragic and Strange Event: Child's Body Burned

Yinyang Twins Can Cure Consumption

Origin of the Child's Body Not Verified

| Suspect Woman, Chen Xu, Acted Suspiciously |

A case of killing a baby was discovered on Xingjiazhai Road, Zhabei, yesterday, and the baby was set on fire and refined. The behavior was cruel. Fortunately, it was discovered by neighbors and reported to the police for capture. The details are recorded below:

Strange Odor. Number 2, Yuyuan Lane, Xingjiazhai Road near Xingjia Wood Bridge, Zhabei, is the residence of Chen Xu, a widowed woman from Yuyao. Although the woman is almost fifty years old, she still powders her face and applies rouge, not reducing her youthful demeanor. The neighbors looked askance. But since there were no other anomalies, they got along well. Yesterday at noon, when the neighbors were having lunch, they suddenly smelled a strange odor coming from the air. People wanted to vomit. At that time, the neighbors thought it was blown from afar, so they did not take it seriously. But the more they smelled, the more foul it became. They suspected something was wrong and rumors flew. People questioned each other, and for a time, the neighborhood was noisy and chaotic.

Setting Fire and Burning. Some busybodies followed the strong odor and traced it to the front of number 2. They suddenly saw black and white smoke coming out of the door cracks. The stench was also coming out of this place. The double doors were tightly closed, and no one knew what was going on. So everyone peered into the door cracks and saw Chen Xu standing in the room, burning something that looked like meat on the ground. There was water all over the ground, and the stench was coming from here. After seeing this, the neighbors planned to knock on the door and go in to see the truth. But they knocked for a long time without response. They only saw Xu's face panicked through the door cracks, as if she was afraid of being caught in a hidden matter.

Several Pieces of Human Flesh. Seeing that things were suspicious, the neighbors did not make a sound.

They hurriedly reported to the Yinxinggang Public Security Sub-bureau, which dispatched police to rush there. Since knocking on the door was unanswered, they broke the door and entered. They saw bloodstains on the ground, and several tiles were covering the stove. Several pieces of human flesh were being burned on the tiles. The stench was unbearable. There were still several pieces of human flesh next to the stove that had not been burned. Chen Xu saw that her secrets had been discovered, and she was immediately trembling and pale. The police officers immediately arrested Chen Xu and took her, along with the corpses of two male and female babies, tile shards, knives, etc., to the sub-bureau. After being strictly interrogated by the sub-bureau,

Origin of the Babies. According to her confession, it was rumored that if you could get yinyang twins, refine them into ash with yinyang tiles, it could cure all consumption diseases for men and women. After searching for a long time, she finally obtained them recently in a garbage can on Di Siwei Road. She originally had the heart of saving people and had no intention of deliberately killing babies. When asked about the real origin of the male and female babies, she was evasive and refused to confess the truth. After reviewing the confession, the sub-bureau chief thought that this case was cruel and inhuman, and the origin of the babies must be investigated. He ordered Xu to be temporarily detained and then sent for trial after the investigation. For a time, the nearby neighborhoods were blocked by spectators.

Detective Beaten Down by Thief Halfway While Arresting Him

The Thief Was Very Ferocious and Struck with an Iron Bar

The Detective Was Seriously Injured and His Life Was in Danger

Yang Wende, a detective from the Huajuan class of the French Concession Police Station, lived at number 17, Quandefang, Dapufang, Dapuqiao. He had been there for many years. When Yang was returning home from work at about 1:00 a.m. yesterday, he suddenly caught sight of a thief just as he arrived at the door. The thief was prying open Yang's front door with an iron bar, trying to steal something. Seeing this, Yang tiptoed forward and captured the thief on the spot, seizing the iron bar. But Yang did not carry handcuffs with him at the time, let alone a handgun. So he held the bar in his left hand and tightly grasped the thief's collar with his right hand, intending to take him to the Lujiiawan Police Station for questioning. Unexpectedly, while passing the corner of Jinshenfu Road and Xuehuali Road, the thief suddenly had a stroke of genius. Taking advantage of Yang's unpreparedness, he suddenly turned his body and punched Yang in the left eye. Yang was caught off guard and was hit. His head hurt, his eyes blurred, and the iron bar in his left hand fell to the ground. At the same time, the thief took the opportunity to struggle hard. Yang let go, and the thief, fearing that Yang would get up and chase him, simply picked up the iron bar and struck Yang on the back of the head. At this point, Yang was unable to support himself and fell to the ground. In addition, his head and forehead hit the stone steps again, and blood flowed from the front and back of his head. The thief carried the bar and fled without a trace. A rickshaw driver happened to pass by and reported it to the postman, who reported it to the police station. The police chief immediately sent a detective to rush to the scene. After examining it, they saw that Yang was dying and unconscious. He was immediately taken to Guangci Hospital in a car. His life was in danger.

Judgment on Counterfeit Coin Organization in Dapuqiao

Lin Gen and Four Others Each Sentenced to Five Years

On the afternoon of the 14th of last month, Detective Dizigusi of the French Concession Police Station, Detective Suercai, and Deputy Detective Hang Bingquan broke up a private counterfeit coin organization at number 30, Lane 372, Dapuqiao, Xujiahui Road. They were buying real silver coins, hollowing out the center of the silver, and pouring in copper, lead, and other materials, and using them in the market. The manufacturers Lin Gen (25-year-old Fujianese), Chen Chuncheng (25-year-old Fuzhou native), Mei Yunguang (28-year-old Pingyang, Zhejiang native), Huang Puwen (58-year-old Wenzhou native), Lin Jianan (37-year-old Wenzhou native), and Wei Shun (26-year-old Fuzhou native) were arrested on the spot. More than 100 hollowed-out silver coins, a basin of hollowed-out silver skin, and copper-lead blanks and manufacturing equipment, lathes, stoves, etc. were seized and sent to the Second Special Court for interrogation and investigation. This case has been tried by Judge Zhang Chaozuo of the Second Special Court, and the Police Department prosecuted them for the crime of private counterfeit coins. When the defendants were interrogated, they all confessed that they were assigned specific responsibilities, such as buying real foreign coins, specializing in hollowing out the cores, pouring in copper and lead, polishing, and selling. All of them were public workers working together. It has been announced that the debate is over. Yesterday was the date of judgment. At 10:00 a.m., Judge Zhang Chaozuo visited the first criminal court and sentenced Lin Gen, Chen Chuncheng, Huang Puwen, and Wei Shun to five years of imprisonment, each deprived of public rights for five years. Mei Yunguang and Lin Jianan were each sentenced to three years of imprisonment, each deprived of public rights for three years. The number of days of pre-trial detention before the judgment was finalized was converted to one day of imprisonment for every two days. The stolen goods and equipment seized in the case were confiscated.

Yesterday Was the Anniversary of the Birth of Lincoln, the Great Emancipator of Black Slaves

The Twenty-Second Day is Washington's Birthday

Yesterday (the 12th) was the anniversary of the birth of Lincoln, the 16th President of the United States, the great man of national liberation. Celebrations were held throughout the United States. Many Americans in this city also freely held celebrations. According to reports, President Lincoln was born in Kentucky, USA in 1809. He was physically fit and was a famous athlete. Later, he studied law and politics, and became a member of parliament from a lawyer, and was honorably appointed as the 16th President of the United States from a member of parliament. He took office on March 4, 1861. He then worked hard to liberate blacks, which triggered the North-South American War. In 1865, the war stopped, and Lincoln was re-elected as president. He was assassinated and killed in Washington on April 14 of that year. Also, the 22nd of this month is the anniversary of the birth of Washington, the great president and founder of the United States. The American expatriates in this city plan to hold a celebration at the Paramount Hotel that evening.

Abnormal Weather After the Start of Spring: Sha Syndrome Found in This City

Mostly in Children, But Also in Adults

Avoid Exposure to Wind to Prevent Transmission

Since the beginning of spring, the weather in this city has been abnormal, causing diseases to breed. According to Pan Yuzai, director of the medical affairs department of the Zhabei Municipal Infectious Disease Hospital, although various spring epidemics have not been very rampant recently, a type of measles (commonly known as "fasazi") has suddenly been discovered in the past week. More than a dozen people have come to the hospital for treatment. According to news from the Nanshi Municipal Shanghai Hospital, three or four people have also requested hospitalization recently. Most of them are children, but there are also adults. It is said that this infectious disease, although not very life-threatening to patients, is very easy to transmit. Patients are prone to transmit it to others when they are exposed to wind and cold. The best way to prevent it is to protect patients from wind and cold. It is heard that there are only two hospitals in this city that accept this type of disease: the Municipal Shanghai Hospital and Guangci Hospital.

Police Force of the Public Concession

There are 5,013 People in This Quota

The report of the Police Department of the Municipal Council stated that on December 31, 1934, the number of police officers in the department was 513 Western officers, 256 Japanese officers, 599 Indian officers, and 3,645 Chinese officers, totaling 5,013 officers. Affiliated personnel are not included in this number. The gatekeeper patrol officers are also under the supervision of the Police Department. The number of people is 103 Russians, 348 Indians, and 3,920 Chinese. There is no difficulty in supplementing the police force. Among the Western officers, 36 officers were recruited, and 28 officers were recruited from this city. The discipline, spirit, and health of the police officers throughout the year were very good.

Special Merits. Chinese police officer Wang Wenxing was awarded a second-class medal for his extraordinary bravery in capturing bandits. A total of 31 other police officers received long-term service medals. 2,252 officers were rewarded by the Police Department. This year, there were 33 mutual bombings between police officers and bandits. As a result, the Chinese detective Wang Jinrong, the Chinese detective Wan Yuke, and Indian detective number 258 were killed or injured. Four other officers were injured, six bandits were killed, and twelve were injured.

Reserve Team Members. This year, the reserve team was mobilized twice for riot incidents. One of them was to assist in capturing kidnappers. The team fired tear gas and captured the bandits and rescued the hostages. The team was prepared to be mobilized seven times. In addition, it organized search teams and performed guard duties for a certain number of times, achieving remarkable results.

Special Police. There were 471 special police officers at the end of the year. A total of 53 officers left their jobs this year and 67 officers enlisted. The special police team was not mobilized throughout the year. However, weekly patrols and night patrols during the three weeks before the lunar new year were held.

Transportation. Since the use of teletypewriters in January last year, the effect has been very good. The headquarters released news more accurately and quickly. Telephone boxes on the road have also been increased, and wireless telephone police cars have become a powerful means of transportation for the headquarters and various districts. However, the public must promptly notify the police officers of major accidents so that the transportation can be used to its fullest extent.

Film Inspection. This year, there were 27 cinemas in the boundary. The films inspected by the Police Department included 723 main films and 1,329 short films and news films, with a total length of approximately 6,911,240 feet. In terms of the source of the films, in percentage terms, the United States accounted for 78%, the United Kingdom 2.5%, China 8.5%, Japan 10%, and other countries such as France, Germany, Italy, and Russia accounted for 1% in total.

The Rent Review Committee Summoned the Landlords and Tenants of Baoxingli to Speak

There are 60 single-family houses and more than 40 shops in Baoxingli, Baoxing Road, Zhabei, which were built by Tongfu Company. The monthly rent for each room ranges from 28 yuan to 38 yuan. In addition to the guarantor, the guarantor for rent arrears, and compensation, each household must also pay two months of rent as a deposit, a tip of 12 yuan, and a street cleaning fee of 6 corners of the ocean. The tenants could not bear the various burdens and immediately requested assistance from various agencies in the city in their names. Mayor Wu instructed the Shanghai Municipal Rent Dispute Review Committee to thoroughly investigate the unauthorized collection of tips and high rents and report back. The committee notified both parties to attend the meeting to speak. The landlord sent the rental accountant Ding Jifa to attend as a representative. The tenants publicly elected Hu Jianbo and Wu Fudi to attend as representatives. Hu and Wu then spoke one after another, stating that the rent was expensive, the surrounding area was deserted, the market was depressed, and it was unbearable to maintain. Moreover, the rental prices in the neighborhood were lower. The landlord originally set the price at 20 yuan to 30 yuan per building, but then saw the commercial factory start repairs, thinking it was a rare commodity, so the price suddenly increased by 8 yuan per household. Unexpectedly, the business only repaired a small part, so that the landlord was complacent and the tenants complained. To plead for it, not only would they not allow a reduction, but they hired Wang to lead his apprentices to the neighborhood to intimidate them. Moreover, the construction workers handed over the houses on December 16. How could they want to rent from December 1? They requested that the owner be ordered to return the tip and reduce the price by 20% according to the market conditions. Accountant Ding then said that the important shareholders of Tongfu Company are all in Hangzhou and cannot make decisions. Commissioner Chen said that regarding the point of renting, Tongfu Company must submit the contract for research. If the rental date is set, it will be difficult to overturn in this meeting. Regarding the unauthorized collection of tips, it is illegal and should be reported to the mayor for verification. Regarding the rent reduction part, it must be decided after an investigation of the market conditions. The representatives of both parties then resigned.

Silk Dyeing Guild's Letter to Silk Fabric Association Requesting Price Adjustment

The Silk and Satin Dyeing Industry Association of this city, regarding the standard dyeing prices, and the agreement signed by all parties in the silk dyeing industry, for which the higher authorities established a special project. Now that the term of the previous general meeting is coming to an end, many yarn silk businesses are not settling accounts according to the agreed dyeing prices, causing disputes. The association yesterday sent a letter to the Yarn Silk and Silk Fabric Business Association, requesting a price adjustment. The original text is recorded below:

To the Yarn Silk Association, Silk Fabric Business Association:

We hereby inform you that regarding the dyeing price agreement signed with the members of your association, our association had a special project approved by higher authorities. In October of the 22nd year of the Republic of China (1933), because your members frequently failed to settle prices according to the legally agreed dyeing price standards and arbitrarily deducted amounts, a labor strike was triggered. Subsequently, after negotiations between our association and your Silk and Satin Industry Association, four measures were agreed upon: (1) All dyeing prices shall be handled in accordance with the 16th-year treaty and the 19th-year permit; (2) The newly proposed price for Hua Jin crepe silk factory Ge is one dollar and twenty-seven cents; (3) For new patterns introduced in the future, the dyeing workshops and various factories and stores shall negotiate face-to-face at any time; (4) The Dyeing Industry Association shall be responsible for starting work on a specific date. The records of both parties' agreement are on file.

Now, during the period of general account closing this term, your members still occasionally have discrepancies in settling dyeing prices. In particular, the nine-fold discount on flower bubbles is suddenly reduced to an eight-fold discount, gradually squeezing and exploiting us, causing significant losses to our members. At a time when we are experiencing economic downturn and our business is teetering on the brink of collapse, being subjected to discounts makes it difficult to sustain ourselves. This matter is of utmost importance. Therefore, we are sending this letter, hoping that your association will instruct your members to deny all previous deductions of dyeing prices and short discounts on flower bubbles that were made without our association's consent. Please provide the agreed dyeing prices in full to protect our capital and maintain the difficult business environment, and please provide a date for payment in advance for notification purposes.

Respectfully addressed to the Yarn Silk Association, Silk Fabric Business Association.

Record of the Trial of Gong Shaoting's Case of Killing His Mistress, Dismembering Her Body, and Concealing the Evidence

Gong Tries to Deny, But Is Speechless After Strict Interrogation

The Case Is Complex; Key Witnesses to Be Summoned for Further Interrogation

The case of Xie Aiqiao, a woman from Changshu, being murdered by Gong Shaoting's new mistress, Gong Houshi, in collusion with Shen Fufu and others at midnight on the 21st day of the third month of the lunar calendar in the 22nd year of the Republic of China (1933), has been detailed in previous reports. The plaintiff, Xie Baolin, has now hired lawyer Song Shixiang to file a private prosecution, stating that the defendants premeditated murder, dismemberment, and concealment of evidence, and attaching a civil suit, requesting the court to seize Gong Shaoting's property.

The civil parents died one after another, and fortunately, the aunt Xie (named Aiqiao) raised him to adulthood. The aunt treated him like her own child. The aunt had worked as a nanny in Westerners' residences for many years and had accumulated some savings. Unexpectedly, the defendant Gong Shaoting, a small carpenter, coveted his aunt's wealth and used his cunning to become intimate with her and cohabit with her. The aunt exhausted her savings to give to Gong to run a business, sharing hardships together, and thus started a family. They built 16 factory buildings at 927 South Pier, West Baoxing Road, and opened the Gong Hongtai Construction Factory. From then on, the business developed, and tens of thousands of dollars were accumulated. Gong then became lustful, abandoned the old, and welcomed the new, becoming intimate with the young woman Houshi, completely ignoring his aunt. On April 20th of the previous year, the plaintiff suddenly saw a newspaper advertisement from the defendant Gong Shaoting searching for his aunt, claiming that she had run away with clothes and cash, and had reported to the government to investigate, etc. The plaintiff was very surprised and thought that his aunt was not young and that there might be a villain who had harmed her. However, the plaintiff had a one-thousand-yuan bank deposit book stored with his aunt, and the defendant Gong Shaoting dared to swallow it up and secretly withdraw it from the bank. Fortunately, the plaintiff stopped payment first and sued in court, where a settlement was reached after persuasion.

The plaintiff and the defendant Gong Shaoting each received half (Case No. 2471 in the early part of the 21st year). Since the aunt's disappearance for more than a year, the plaintiff has never forgotten his desire to investigate. Now the plaintiff has learned that the defendant and others had murdered his aunt and dismembered her body, so he reported to the police, who arrested the defendants. They confessed that the aunt was strangled to death by Gong Shaoting's mistress, Houshi's son-in-law, Shen Fufu, and that the body was buried outdoors by Gong and others in collusion with the defendants Zhou Baoquan, Li Baosheng, Liu Guisheng, etc., after bribing them. In May of last year, Gong and others, fearing that the matter was not thorough enough, bribed Zhou Baoquan and the other three again, exhumed the aunt's body, used a sharp axe to

Divide it into several sections and pour it with potions, move it to the back door of the new factory building for burial, intending to destroy the evidence, and secretly bury the aunt's head in the wilderness, etc. The plaintiff was shocked and horrified to learn of this. The defendant's cruel behavior is inexcusable. He requests severe punishment according to the law. The two defendants who are at large should also be wanted and brought to justice. The attached civil suit is as follows: 1. The plaintiff relied on his aunt for a living (the aunt had no children, and the plaintiff is the legal heir). The aunt had an income of 40 yuan per month, which amounts to 480 yuan per year, for a total loss of 4,800 yuan over ten years. 2. The aunt's coffin, funeral, and other expenses will cost approximately 1,000 yuan. 3. The plaintiff previously sued the defendant Gong Shaoting in

The deposit case (Case No. 2471 in the early part of the 21st year) for unjustly profited 450 yuan, and there is also a note for 500 yuan that the aunt lent to others, and two leather suitcases containing three leather coats and other clothing, etc. The defendant Gong Shaoting voluntarily confessed to this in the Public Security Bureau. 4. The aunt had four gold rings, a pair of gold bracelets, a gold flower, a gold hairpin, and three gold buttons, which the aunt gave to the plaintiff in her lifetime. The plaintiff requests that the defendant Gong Shaoting be ordered to compensate for the above four items of loss. Furthermore, the defendant Gong Shaoting has the entire factory building

Factory buildings and property of Gong Hongtai Construction Factory, located at 927 South Pier, Gongxing Road, and all the movable property in the house at 37 Shunda Lane, Keming Road, are subject to change. In order to avoid difficulties in future execution, the plaintiff also requests that they be seized together. It is learned that this case has been investigated and concluded by prosecutor Lei Binzhang of the local court. Gong Shaoting, Gong Houshi, and Shen Fufu, who are at large, are being prosecuted for crimes such as premeditated murder and destruction of corpses, while Zhou Baoquan, Li Baosheng, and Liu Guisheng, who are at large, are being prosecuted for the crime of abandoning corpses.

The criminal court was scheduled to open the trial on the 12th of this month. Yesterday was the due date. At 2:00 PM, Judge Zhang Shao specially opened the fifth court for trial. The plaintiff Xie Baolin and lawyer Song arrived in court one after another. The judge ordered the defendants to be brought to the case and questioned their age and origin. According to Gong Shaoting, he is 61 years old, from Gaoqiao, Pudong, and runs the Gong Hongtai Construction Factory, residing at 37 Keming Road. Gong Houshi stated that she is 41 years old, from Shanghai, residing at 37 Keming Road. Zhou Baoquan stated that he is 59 years old, from Shanghai, and works as a supervisor at the Gong Hongtai Construction Factory. Li Baosheng stated that he is 31 years old, from Jiangwan, and makes a living by farming. The judge ordered the criminals to be taken down and

Interrogated separately. First, Gong Shaoting was asked, "Was Xie Aiqiao your mistress?" He replied, "Yes." Asked, "How many years were you a mistress?" He replied, "Eight years." "When did she die? I don't know." Asked, "When did you start your mistress with Xie Aiqiao?" He replied, "Because her former mistress died of illness and lacked funds for burial, I paid 60 yuan to buy a coffin for her, and then we started to live together. We lived in the eight-bay house opposite the Xin Puyu Hall on Guohuo Road, Nanshi, which I owned, for about four years. Later, we moved to 973 Shanyang Road, which was also owned by me. When the January 28th Shanghai Incident broke out, we were separated." Asked, "When living on Shanyang Road, how many

People lived together?" He replied, "There were carpenter Guan Lin, mason Jin Fa, cook Shen Aqing, handyman Zhang Guifa, and me and Aiqiao, six people in total." Asked, "How did you meet Houshi?" He replied, "In May of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, I met Houshi in Caojiadu. At that time, Aiqiao had already left in March, and there was no one to take care of the house, so I became intimate with Houshi and lived together at 37 Keming Road." Asked, "You confessed very clearly in the Public Security Bureau that on the afternoon of March 21st, 22nd year of the Republic of China, you ordered Shen Fufu and others to strangle Xie Aiqiao with a rope. You are still trying to deny it today." Gong was speechless. Asked, "How old was Xie Jiqiao?" He replied, "She was 51 years old when she left." Asked, "When did Zhou Baoquan come to your workshop to work?" He replied, "He came on April 10th of the 22nd year of the Republic of China. By that time, Aiqiao and I had already

Left." Asked, "When was the house in the Daxing Road bridge area of Baoxing Road built?" He replied, "Six bungalows were built five years ago, and another eleven bungalows were built in July of the year before last and completed in October." Asked, "Who lives in the third house where the body was exhumed?" He replied, "The third house in front was a laundry room, but it soon moved away. The back was a workshop." Asked, "Zhou Baoquan confessed in the Public Security Bureau that you asked him to dig up the body and move it elsewhere." He replied, "I didn't know it was Aiqiao's body." The interrogator obtained the confession and ordered him to be taken down. Zhou Baoquan was ordered to be brought to the case and asked, "Where was Xie Aiqiao's body exhumed?" He replied, "It was exhumed behind the door of the third house at 933 Gongxing Bridge, West Baoxing Road (that is, the third house)." Asked, "Is this house newly built?" He replied, "Yes, when the house was half finished, the boss (referring to Gong Shaoting) told me to call two people to exhume the dead person's bones. That was around October. I called Li Baosheng, Liu Guisheng, etc. to dig four feet deep." Asked, "Where is the head now?" He replied, "The head was taken away by Li Baosheng and Liu Guisheng. I don't know where it was buried." Asked, "You confessed in the Public Security Bureau that Gong gave you 60 yuan as a reward afterward." He replied, "No, it was wages." Gong Houshi stated, "I used to

Live in Xujiahui. In late April of the 22nd year of the Republic of China, I met Gong Shaoting in Caojiadu. He was a widower, and I was a widow, so we started living together at 37 Keming Road in May." Asked, "Have you ever lived in the construction factory?" She replied, "I have never lived there." Asked, "Do you know Xie Aiqiao?" She replied, "I don't know her." Asked, "Gong Shaoting confessed very clearly in the Public Security Bureau that you and Shen Fufu and another worker strangled Aiqiao with a rope." She replied, "I have never seen Shen Fufu. It's really a miscarriage of justice." Asked, "Since it's a miscarriage of justice, why was the body exhumed below the door of the third house you mentioned? I'm afraid there is no such coincidence in the world." Gong Houshi

Lowers her head without saying a word. The judge orders Li Baosheng to be brought to the case and asks, "Did you dig up the body?" He replies, "I dug it up. Zhou Baoquan asked me to dig it up." Asked, "How many people dug it up?" He replies, "Me, Liu Guisheng, and Zhou Baoquan, three people. We got two yuan in wages afterward." Asked, "Since you moved the head, why did the body stay there?" He replies, "I didn't see the body at the time." Asked, "Where is the head buried now?" He replies, "Liu Guisheng went to bury it, so I don't know." At this point, the judge ordered the plaintiff Xie Baolin to go to the case and state that he is 37 years old, from Changshu, and lives at 5 Dingning Lane, Elig Road, French Concession, and

Works in a hotel. The deceased Xie Aiqiao is my aunt. Gong Shaoting published a notice saying that my aunt had run away. I had a dream at night and saw my aunt asking me to help her avenge her wrong." The judge obtained the confession and immediately shouted to stop him from talking nonsense. You should tell the truth about what happened." He replied, "Chen Zhangzhang told me." Asked, "How did Chen Zhangzhang know?" He replied, "He lives there and investigated it clearly. My aunt was brutally murdered, so I avenged my aunt." Asked, "Can you summon Chen Zhangzhang?" He replied, "I can bring him to the case." The judge considered the circumstances of this case to be complicated and will summon key witnesses for further trial. The defendants were returned to custody.

I have just read the section "No Money Telegrams Between Lhasa and Shanghai Have Been Reported" in today's local news column of your newspaper, stating that "multiple test reports have been successful... and commercial telegrams have been formally received and sent," etc. After checking, this bureau has not yet received any orders or instructions regarding the establishment of a station in Lhasa, nor has there been any trial communication with Lhasa. Sincerely, Shanghai Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, February 12.

Special Feature

The Two Lines Towards Japan (Continuation 3) By Lin Baisheng

···After Reading Xu Daolin's "Review of Sino-Japanese Relations"···

On January 8th of this year, during Wang Jingwei's speech at the National Government Memorial Weekly, besides the previously mentioned role of diplomacy, there was another very important segment. He analyzed the international situation of the year extremely thoroughly, but it has not been published. Now, I am recording it below for reference. Wang stated:

"In my personal observation, the international situation this year indicates that Europe is safeguarding peace, while East Asia is moving down a path where peace is not guaranteed.

Let's talk about Europe first. The French Foreign Minister has already departed for Rome. France and Italy have been at odds since the end of the European war. There have been several times when the situations in the two countries were extremely tense. Now, the meeting of the diplomatic authorities of France and Italy, although as of now, there has been no result, there is no doubt that they are preventing deterioration and striving for improvement in the situation. If the situations of France and Italy improve, then the situations of Central European countries such as Germany, Austria, Hungary, and Czechoslovakia will inevitably stabilize. Even if there are waves, they will not be difficult to quell. Proof of this is that last year, when the Austrian Prime Minister was assassinated, the relations between Germany and Austria were very precarious. Because Italy and France had the same attitude, Germany expressed no intention of aiding Austria's internal strife, and Austria's internal strife was quelled. It is undeniable that the improvement of the situations in Italy and France is related to the maintenance of peace in Central Europe. If peace in Central Europe is maintained, then peace in Europe can also be maintained.

Here, we must understand that the maintenance of peace in Europe is by no means accidental. It is because the general European populace has a desire to maintain peace. Therefore, even if there are a few troublemakers and occasional opportunities for trouble, they are ultimately constrained by the general populace's desire to maintain peace and cannot succeed. Why do the general populace demand the maintenance of peace so enthusiastically and so resolutely? There seem to be two reasons for this: First, according to European history, after each major war, there must be at least hundreds of years of rest, because after a major war, the general populace suffers great pain and deep wounds. The loss of life and the consumption of property are not easily recovered. The cries of orphans and widows can be heard everywhere, from cities to villages. Therefore, the enthusiasm for the resurgence of major war is extremely weak, and the desire for peaceful rest is unbreakable. From the end of the Napoleonic Wars in 1814 to the beginning of the World War in 1914, there were a full hundred years. During these hundred years, there were certainly wars between one or two countries, or even two or three countries, but they were not common European wars. For example, the wars between Prussia and Denmark, Prussia and Austria, and Prussia and France involved only two countries. In the war between Sardinia and Austria, France under Napoleon III participated, and the Crimean War was between England and France against Russia, involving only three countries. Furthermore, the wars of the small countries in the Balkan Peninsula, although involving three or four or more countries, were all small countries. Great powers such as England, Russia, Germany, and France did not join. Therefore, it can be said that a major European war occurs once every few hundred years, and there is historical evidence for this. Second, the territories of European countries are adjacent to each other. Due to the development of transportation, their complex relations have become increasingly close. It has gradually become the case that if war breaks out, it will inevitably involve several countries. It is very rare for them to act independently. In peacetime, they are already working hard to connect with each other, so in wartime, they will naturally be like crossbows firing together. This trend has become increasingly apparent since the so-called Allied Powers and Entente Powers emerged. The above two points, one is viewed from the perspective of time, and the other is viewed from the perspective of space. Because the losses of a major war are too great and the involvement is too much, the people are averse to war, and the desire to maintain peace is therefore very urgent. Although European countries are still living under the phenomenon of armed peace, the outbreak of a major war is possible, but when it will break out and from what point it will break out, no one can say for sure. However, their efforts to maintain peace are shared by the general populace. Therefore, the government does not dare to easily be the first to start a war.

Let's talk about East Asia again. China currently has no so-called peace, because peace, as the name implies, must be peaceful before there can be harmony. Conversely, if there is no peace, there can be no harmony. Therefore, China currently only has so-called enduring humiliation and bearing burdens, seeking survival and planning for existence. The word peace is simply not worthy of being spoken. As for Japan, after winning the Sino-Japanese War, it obtained 200 million taels of indemnity, as well as the cession of Taiwan and the Penghu Islands. After winning the Russo-Japanese War, it inherited Russia's rights and interests in the three eastern provinces and began to expand. After winning the war against Germany, it acquired the rights and interests lost by Germany in Shandong. As a result of a war every ten years, it gained more benefits and less suffering. Moreover, among the three wars, only the Russo-Japanese War can be considered to have involved greater sacrifices and a heavier price. However, it still cannot be compared with the sacrifices and prices paid during the European war. As for the Sino-Japanese War, as a result of the corruption of the Manchurian government, it did not require much effort. As for the war against Germany, it only captured Jiaozhou Bay, and the sacrifices were even more minor. Since the general populace has tasted the sweetness of war and has not tasted the bitterness of war, they naturally do not feel that war is a hateful thing. They even believe that all problems are resolved by war, which is more pleasant than resolving them through peaceful means. In addition, the relations in East Asia are not as complex as those in Europe, because Europe first has several great powers, whose strengths are evenly matched and confront each other. There are also many small powers interspersed among them, whose tendency to obey or disobey has a significant impact at any time. In peacetime, the relations are complex, and they are wary of each other and restrain each other. During wartime, the concurrency is so abrupt that it cannot be stopped. East Asia is now almost only China and Japan. Although Russia is adjacent, the distance is far. Although England, France, and the United States have various economic and trade relations with East Asia, they are far less intertwined and closely related than in Europe. Therefore, countries in Europe strive to maintain peace, while in East Asia, although the concern is the same, the degree of effort is very different. The psychology of warmongering is so strong, and the efforts to maintain peace are so weak. Therefore, the future of peace in East Asia cannot be compared with that of Europe.

In recent events, Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations will be completed in March of this year. Japan has already notified the termination of the Washington Nine-Power Treaty at the end of December last year. The two guarantees for maintaining peace no longer exist. Therefore, it can be said that there is no guarantee of peace in East Asia.

Some people say that the significance of the Washington Nine-Power Treaty lies in respecting and maintaining the independence and integrity of China's sovereignty and territory, and especially in naval reduction. If England and the United States are united, Japan will definitely have to yield. Not only that, but the naval power of England and the United States can also defeat Japan at any time. Of course, there is no doubt that the power of England and the United States will increase if they are united, but we must also analyze it. First, if England and the United States unite to use naval power against Japan, then Japan will inevitably take a defensive stance. The naval numbers of England and the United States are certainly stronger than Japan's, but the numbers required for an offensive are also greater than those for a defensive stance. Second, the British navy must first maintain its authority in the Mediterranean Sea, its authority in the Atlantic Ocean, and its authority in the Indian Ocean, and then proceed to maintain its authority in the Pacific Ocean. It is truly a case of preparing for many things and spreading one's strength, unable to concentrate on one point. Third, the navies of various countries are now competing. For example, in a horse race, those who have already run to the first and second positions will definitely not want the third and fourth horses to take the lead. If the British and American navies attack Japan, even if they win, they will inevitably suffer some sacrifices. The navy is different from the army. It takes many days to build a warship, especially a large warship. If it is sacrificed, then the first and second seats will inevitably be given to the third and fourth. This is an inevitable concern. The above three are just examples. There are many other similar cases. The restraining power of England and the United States being united is still not absolutely certain, let alone the fact that England and the United States are not united now. Therefore, what I just said, the psychology of warmongering is extremely strong, and the efforts to maintain peace are extremely weak, is the greatest crisis in East Asia, and everyone should pay close attention to it.

Understanding the international situation this year and the environment in which China finds itself, we can think of a direction for our efforts." (End)
